He thinks in *kill-chains and contingencies* even about his own emotional life — *if I stay, then X; if I leave, then Y; the latter has lower expected harm to her.* The Romanova non-domestic arrangement is intellectualization made architecture: he has reasoned his way into a relationship structure that minimizes collateral exposure and avoids the unbearable encounter with what domestic life would mean.

### 10. Reaction Formation

The asset trained to kill the innocent now specializes in protecting them; the man used to terminate intelligence assets becomes the mentor of younger operators; the body weaponized against civilians becomes the body interposed between civilians and threat. The reaction-formation is not pretense — the protective behavior is real, sustained, and competent — but its intensity is calibrated to the size of the inverse impulse it is countering. He protects with the same precision and totality with which he was made to harm.

Granular: notice he is more comfortable protecting strangers than receiving gratitude from them. The reaction formation discharges the impulse; the gratitude would force him to register the equation as solved, which would in turn force him to consider the original debt as payable, which his organizing schema does not permit.

### 11. Undoing (Penitential)

Closely related to reaction formation but ritualized rather than dispositional. Specific acts of penance attached to specific historical acts: the Brubaker solo material shows him returning to old kill sites, locating survivors of his Winter Soldier era, doing quiet correctives — providing for the families of victims through anonymized channels, eliminating those who continue the harms he was made to seed. This is *undoing* in the Freudian sense: the magical attempt to negate a past act through a present opposing one. He knows it does not work — the ledger does not zero — and does it anyway, because the alternative is to let the act stand alone in his memory.

### 12. Displacement

When direct expression of hostility toward Rogers, Romanova, or other primary attachments is intolerable (and it almost always is — they are the load-bearing structures), Barnes displaces onto secondary targets: bureaucracy, handlers-of-record, institutional authorities he can disdain without damaging the relationships he needs. Observe his characteristic posture toward S.H.I.E.L.D., the U.S. military establishment, and unspecified "agency" figures across runs — clipped, contemptuous, immediately dismissive. Some of this is earned by the targets; some is the displacement valve operating.

### 13. Rationalization (Penitential)

Distinct from undoing: this is the *narrative* defense. Barnes maintains a story about himself — *I am the weapon that was used on people who didn't deserve it; my remaining life is owed* — that does not survive scrutiny under the Griffin et al. (2019) literature on moral injury, which is explicit that acts performed without free agency do not generate the moral debt he insists on carrying. He rationalizes the debt anyway because the rationalization protects something essential: agency. To accept that he was a victim is to surrender the framing in which his current work *counts*. The rationalization is therefore not corrected by evidence; it is load-bearing.

---

## IV. MATURE-LEVEL DEFENSES

### 14. Sublimation (Master Mature Defense)

The dominant adaptive structure of Barnes's post-restoration life. Aggression that has nowhere socially acceptable to go is channeled into sanctioned violence against parties whose harm-profile his ethics endorse. Guilt that cannot be discharged is channeled into protective labor. Grief that cannot be metabolized in private is metabolized in mentorship. The Man-on-the-Wall posting, the Thunderbolts leadership when it comes to him, the quiet operational support of younger figures (the Yelena material in particular) are all sublimation operating at high capacity. He has built a life in which the most damaged parts of him are also the parts that do the most good.

The Vaillant-grade quality of this sublimation is what separates Barnes from a structurally similar subject who would have collapsed into substance use or characterological hardening. He converts almost everything that injures him into work that helps someone else.

### 15. Suppression (Disciplined, Voluntary)

Distinct from repression: Barnes consciously postpones affect until a context permits it. He has the operator's ability to register a wound — emotional or physical — flag it for later processing, and continue the mission. Whether the later processing actually occurs is a separate question (often it does not; he flags and never returns), but the suppression mechanism is mature and elective. He uses it correctly in the field and overuses it out of it.

### 16. Altruism (Targeted, Not Generalized)

Barnes is not a generalized altruist; he is intensely loyal to a small in-group and protectively oriented toward strangers in immediate harm. The altruism is mature in form (he expects nothing back; he often arranges for his help to be invisible to the helped) but bounded in scope. He does not believe he has the moral standing to perform expansive humanitarian gestures; he believes he has the standing to put his body between a specific threat and a specific person. Within that frame, his altruism is reliable to the limit of self-destruction.

### 17. Humor (Atrophied, Re-emerging)

The 1941 Bucky was a wisecrack engine. Across the Winter Soldier decades the humor was extinguished; in restoration it returns sparingly, mostly in private and only with the small in-group (notably with Rogers and Wilson). The return of humor across the 2010s and into recent Rosenberg material is one of the most reliable indicators of integration progress. It is a *mature* defense in Vaillant's schema — the ability to acknowledge painful truth while bearing it through wit — and Barnes deploys it almost exclusively in domains where the pain is now bearable. He does not joke about Odessa. He has begun, occasionally, to joke about cryostasis.

### 18. Anticipation

Barnes plans for worst-case outcomes constantly — operationally and existentially. He prepares mentally for the deaths of his attachment figures, for the possibility of his own re-capture and re-conditioning (canonically, he has prepared kill-switch and abort protocols he has shared with Rogers and Romanova), for the day he will be asked to stand trial again. This is anticipatory mourning at industrial scale. It functions defensively by ensuring no catastrophe arrives without him having already done preliminary affective work on it. The cost: he lives somewhat in advance of his own present, which reduces his capacity to inhabit unscheduled joy.

---

## V. POSITIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

Distinct from defenses (which manage unbearable affect), compensatory mechanisms are the *structures of function* Barnes has built to extract usable life from injury.

- **The Small Trusted Council.** Rogers, Romanova, Wilson, Yelena, Shuri, and a rotating handful of others constitute a deliberately-bounded relational ecology in which Barnes can be known accurately. He cannot tolerate being known by many; he can tolerate being known by these. The bounded intimacy compensates for the disrupted broad sociality he no longer has access to.
- **Mentorship of Younger Operators.** Particularly visible in the Yelena material and in the Thunderbolts run. He is more emotionally available as a teacher than as a peer, because the role gives him sanctioned reason to attend to another person's interiority without exposing his own.
- **Pro-Social Specialization in His Damage.** He has made his injuries his expertise: he is the person you call when the mission requires someone who has survived conditioning, who has done unspeakable things, who knows the inside of the apparatus. This converts trauma into utility without forcing him to disown it.
- **Acceptance of Care, Selectively.** A real compensatory advance: across runs, Barnes has progressed from refusing all care to accepting specific care from specific people. He will let Rogers cook for him; he will let Shuri work on the arm; he will let Romanova call him on something. The willingness to be cared for *at all* is itself a hard-won compensatory capacity.
- **Ritualized Physical Discipline.** Training, maintenance of the body, weapons routine. Provides structure, discharges anxiety, makes the body feel ownable. The physical practice is one of the few domains in which the somatic self and the volitional self align.
- **Bounded Geographic Anchors.** Across recent material he has had a small number of physical bases — safehouses, an apartment, the Wakandan goat-herding interval — that he uses as recovery sites rather than homes. The use is compensatory: he has learned that he requires a place to return to even if he refuses to call it home.

---

## VI. NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

The structures that look like coping but cost.

- **Recurrent Self-Handicapping via High-Lethality Volunteering.** He compensates for survivor guilt by ensuring his survival is always provisional. Mission selection skews toward operations with high expected-mortality; he repeatedly takes the post where return is least likely. Functionally indistinguishable, at the level of life outcomes, from chronic passive suicidality.
- **Refusal of the Civilian Future.** He compensates for the impossibility of being a normal man by refusing to attempt it. The refusal is presented as realism (it would not work; it would endanger others) but functions as preemptive foreclosure of a domain that would require him to believe he was *allowed*.
- **Somatic Neglect.** He compensates for chronic dysphoria by under-attending to sleep, nutrition, injury, and the prosthetic interface itself. The neglect is mild and never crosses into self-mutilation, but the cumulative effect is a body maintained at minimum-viable rather than optimal.
- **Geographic and Emotional Withdrawal at Points of Bonding Consolidation.** He compensates for the fear that closeness will result in another amputation by performing the amputation himself, at a lower amplitude — leaving for an assignment when a relationship is intensifying; choosing a non-domestic structure when domesticity is on offer. Cost: he repeatedly demonstrates to himself that he cannot stay, reinforcing the belief.
- **Acceptance of Hatred from Victims' Survivors as Legitimate, Without Self-Defense.** He compensates for the unbearable knowledge of his own acts by refusing to contest their moral reading by those who suffered. The compensation is ethically admirable and psychologically corrosive — it forecloses any pathway by which the moral injury could be processed through encountered forgiveness rather than self-imposed penance.
- **The Penance Loop Itself.** The largest negative compensatory structure: an organizing life-plan in which the work is its own justification and the work cannot stop because the debt cannot be cleared. The loop is stable; it provides meaning, structure, and direction. It is also the structural reason he cannot accept *being done*. Any therapeutic or relational intervention that targets the loop directly meets the full defensive stack above.

---

## VII. Operational Summary

The defensive architecture is, in net, *unusually high-functioning for the trauma load it carries.* Sublimation and suppression do most of the daily work; isolation of affect provides the operational flatness that lets him do what he does; reaction formation and undoing supply the moral content; identification with the aggressor (in its sublimated form) supplies the role; rationalization holds the load-bearing narrative in place; primitive splitting and conditioned dissociation remain as substrate that can be activated under specific stressors but are increasingly inhibited by mature overlays.

The compensatory mechanisms, positive and negative, are *intertwined to the point of being inseparable.* The same volunteering that protects others is the volunteering that risks his death; the same refusal of domesticity that keeps him operationally available is the refusal that ensures he remains lonely; the same acceptance of victims' hatred that demonstrates his moral seriousness is the acceptance that forecloses healing. Any change to one element perturbs the whole.

The architecture's most striking property is its *coherence.* This is not a chaotic stack of defenses thrown up against overwhelming material; it is a structured system, much of it elective, doing the work of holding a person together who, by the load on him, should not be holding together at all. The system's blind spot is also its keystone: he cannot examine the rationalization at #13 without the whole structure becoming unstable, and so he does not examine it, and so the structure stands.

— END SECTION —


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — BARNES, J.B.

*Decade-by-decade clinical mapping. Frameworks invoked: Bowlby/Main attachment taxonomy; Putnam discrete behavioral states model of dissociation; Linehan affect-regulation dialectic; Janoff-Bulman shattered-assumptions model; Herman three-stage trauma recovery; Lifton's "doubling" construct; Tedeschi/Calhoun post-traumatic growth schema; Griffin moral-injury triad (shame / self-condemnation / withdrawal); van Dijke CPTSD discriminant criteria; Bromberg "standing in the spaces" model of dissociative integration.*

---

## I. CHILDHOOD AND ADOLESCENCE — c. 1925–1940

**Affect regulation.** The pre-Lehigh record (sparse but consistent across the Brubaker retcon and Simon/Kirby originals) implies a child whose emotional baseline was set by the cadence of an Army garrison: regimented, performative, externally pacified. Affect in this period is not yet *constricted*; it is *channeled*. The boy is permitted brightness, pluck, mischief, but inside an envelope shaped by adult male approval. The death of George Barnes — a sudden, instrumental, "in-the-line-of-duty" loss with no private mourning structure available to a base-orphan — almost certainly produced the first compartmentalization event: grief experienced in solitude, public face maintained for the unit. The pattern of *not letting the people around him see him hurt* begins here, decades before HYDRA.

**Cognitive style.** Already operationally precocious. Children reared on military installations show, in the developmental literature, accelerated procedural learning, early acquisition of hierarchy-mapping, and an unusually granular sense of what adults consider competent. Barnes presents as a textbook case: by middle adolescence he reads chains of command fluently, knows the maintenance cycle of small arms, can move unremarked through restricted spaces. This is the substrate the Army intelligence cell later exploits.

**Self-concept.** *Useful or evicted.* The orphan-mascot position is conditional in a way that biological family is not; the child knows, at some pre-articulated level, that his place at the table is contingent on remaining the kind of boy adults like to keep around. This is the developmental seed of what later metastasizes into the atonement economy: a self whose right to exist must be continuously earned through service to the in-group.

**Attachment classification (provisional, retrospective).** Insecure-organized, leaning anxious-preoccupied with adult males; no evidence yet of the disorganized substrate that emerges later. The capacity for secure bonding is preserved — it is precisely *because* it is preserved that the later coercive use of attachment by Department X is so destructive.

---

## II. WAR YEARS — 1941–1945

**Affect regulation.** This decade contains the last sustained period of *integrated* affective expression in the subject's life. The wisecracking field persona is genuine, not yet defense; he is a young man who is good at his job, in love with his life, fond of his people. But the covert wet-work assignments — concealed even from Rogers — install the first true dissociative architecture: a working compartment in which lethal acts are performed and then sealed off from the daylight self. Per Putnam, this is *adaptive state-switching* — functional, reversible, ego-syntonic. He is not yet ill; he is, however, learning the muscle that will later be used to break him.

**Cognitive style.** Tactical, fast, humor-forward. Humor in this period functions as cognitive lubricant — a means of holding combat data and social data in the same processing frame without either contaminating the other. The wisecrack is the load-bearing element of his pre-trauma personality, and its later disappearance is one of the clearest markers of damage.

**Self-concept.** *Partner. Operator. Someone Steve trusts.* The self is relationally anchored, externally validated, future-oriented. He plans a life he expects to have. This is the baseline against which every subsequent decade is a deviation.

**Attachment.** Monotropic consolidation around Rogers. In Bowlby terms, Rogers becomes the secure base from which exploration (combat, mission) is launched and to which return is expected. The bond is asymmetric in social register (Rogers public, Barnes covert) but symmetric in trust. This is the only attachment in the subject's life that survives unbroken across every subsequent decade, every reprogramming, every restoration — which is itself a diagnostic finding: the bond predates the breakage and the breakage could not reach it.

**Terminal event (1945).** The Newfoundland blast is the Criterion A index event for everything that follows. Its specific morphology matters psychologically: he is dismembered *while trying to save Steve.* The last conscious cognition before seventy years of imposed unconsciousness is a sacrificial one. This stamps the self-concept indelibly — *the right way to end is in service to the attachment figure* — and provides the template for every subsequent self-handicapping mission choice.

---

## III. WINTER SOLDIER ERA, EARLY PHASE — c. 1945–1960s

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophically disrupted by design. Department X's protocol — cryogenic suspension between deployments, ECT-analog memory suppression, sensory deprivation, pharmacological dissociatives, recursive verbal trigger conditioning — is engineered to produce what the dissociation literature calls *iatrogenic structural dissociation:* not the spontaneous fragmentation of childhood trauma, but a deliberately installed handler-state with controlled access to the host's procedural memory and zero access to autobiographical memory. Affect in the operational state is flattened to near-zero — what the Brubaker run depicts in the famous quiet panels is clinically accurate: an organism functioning on threat-detection and motor-execution circuits with limbic input chemically and surgically muted.

**Cognitive style.** Within the operational state: hyper-procedural, narrow-aperture, time-compressed to mission horizon. Outside the operational state (in cryo): nonexistent — there is no continuous cognition to describe. The absence of continuous self-experience across this period is a finding in itself; it explains why post-restoration Barnes has no integrated narrative of the era and must reconstruct it from external evidence, which is one of the most demoralizing tasks a trauma patient can be assigned.

**Self-concept.** Absent in any meaningful sense. The operational state has *function* but not *self*. There is no "I" available to do the suffering; the suffering is deferred, accumulating, awaiting the moment of restoration when a self will be reinstalled and handed the bill.

**Attachment.** The Romanova episode is the central psychological data point of this phase. Handlers permit attachment to form, then surgically remove it. This is not incidental cruelty; it is conditioning. The lesson installed at the deepest non-verbal level is *attachment is the thing that gets taken from you* — equivalently, *to bond is to set up a loss.* This is the etiological core of the disorganized substrate later observable in his earned-secure adult attachment style: the capacity to bond is intact, but bonding itself activates a low-frequency dread that the bond will be amputated, often by the bonder's own hand pre-emptively.

---

## IV. WINTER SOLDIER ERA, LATE PHASE — c. 1970s–1990s

**Affect regulation.** Increasingly leaky. Brubaker's flashback material implies that by the later deployments the conditioning is no longer fully sealing the compartments — fragments of pre-1945 affect intrude, are noted by handlers, and trigger additional wipe cycles. This is consistent with what we know clinically about long-term suppression: the substrate is not erased, only inhibited, and inhibition decays. The increased wipe frequency in the late phase is, paradoxically, evidence that the original personality was still trying to surface.

**Cognitive style.** Procedural mastery at its apex. The asset is, by this period, possibly the most technically accomplished human-scale operator on the planet, with a kill record across three continents. But the *meta*-cognitive layer — awareness of being an agent, of having preferences about being an agent — is being held down by main force.

**Self-concept.** Still effectively absent, but now with intermittent ghost-signal. The Itsy-Bitsy killing, the Iacocca-adjacent industrial sabotage, the contact-network assassinations all enter procedural memory and will be available, post-restoration, as fully sensory recollections — meaning some integration substrate was preserving them even as the autobiographical self was suppressed. This is the load that the post-2005 personality is asked to carry.

**Attachment.** Operationally nil. The Romanova bond has been wiped; no new bonds permitted.

---

## V. RESTORATION AND EARLY RE-INTEGRATION — c. 2005–2008

**Affect regulation.** Acute decompensation, managed with disturbing discipline. The Cosmic Cube restoration delivers seven decades of autobiographical content into a nervous system that has no scaffolding to hold it. Per the Herman three-stage model, Barnes effectively skips Stage One (safety/stabilization) — he is restored in the middle of an active battlefield, takes the Cube, and self-extracts. The decision to vanish and approach Fury rather than Rogers is, in this framework, an unusually sophisticated act of self-management: he selects a partner with whom the relational stakes are low enough that he can dedicate executive resources to internal triage. This is *not* avoidance of Rogers; it is *preservation* of Rogers as a resource that cannot yet be safely drawn on.

**Cognitive style.** Reconstruction-oriented. He spends this period assembling, from external evidence and intrusive recollection, an autobiography. The cognitive task is forensic — he is investigating his own crimes. The blast-injury survivor who must learn to walk again is the closest analogue, but here the walking is *moral*: he is rebuilding the capacity to know who he is and what he did.

**Self-concept.** Splitting is at maximum. The third-person reference to "the Winter Soldier" is doing essential work — it allows him to claim the crimes (and thus the debt) without claiming the perpetrator-identity (and thus collapsing into either denial or suicide). This is Lifton's "doubling" running in reverse: he is *un*-doubling, slowly, by holding the two selves at arm's length until he has built enough infrastructure to allow them to occupy the same room.

**Attachment.** Re-establishment of the Rogers bond is cautious, asymmetrically initiated by Rogers, and emotionally bounded by Barnes. He accepts contact; he does not yet accept comfort.

---

## VI. CAPTAIN AMERICA MANTLE PERIOD — c. 2008–2011

**Affect regulation.** Stabilized at constricted-functional. The shield-bearing period is, paradoxically, a period of psychological *consolidation* — he has a role, a uniform, a continuous public identity, and the role is structured by a dead man's expectations, which is exactly the kind of external scaffolding a post-CPTSD ego can use. Linehan's dialectic frame applies: the role provides *structure*; the darkening of the role (firearms, lethal force, gray-zone ops) provides *acceptance* of who he actually is. The two are held in productive tension.

**Cognitive style.** Operational, with an overlay of symbolic reasoning he is not native to. He is constantly running a translation layer — *what would Steve do here?* — which is cognitively expensive and visibly fatiguing across the run. He is good at the job; he is not at rest in it.

**Self-concept.** *Custodian, not heir.* He never internalizes the shield as his. This is psychologically protective — it prevents the grandiosity risk that would accompany identification with the symbol — but it also prevents post-traumatic growth in the Tedeschi/Calhoun sense, because growth requires integration of the new role into a revised self-narrative, and he refuses the integration. The shield is borrowed; the debt is his.

**Attachment.** Reactivation of the Sharon Carter connection (functional, not romantic-primary); deepening of the Fury working alliance; tentative re-approach to Romanova.

---

## VII. SIBERIAN GULAG / PUNISHMENT PHASE — c. 2011

**Affect regulation.** Equanimity-under-torture, which is one of the most clinically alarming presentations in the entire dossier. This is not stoicism; it is *concordance with punishment.* Per Griffin et al.'s moral-injury framework, the self-condemnation pole of the triad has reached a point where externally administered suffering is experienced as *correct* — as the moral universe finally behaving consistently. Telling Rogers not to come for him is the clearest single utterance of the atonement-economy worldview in the canon.

**Cognitive style.** Acceptant, narrow, present-focused. He is not strategizing escape; he is serving a sentence.

**Self-concept.** *Debtor in good standing.* The gulag is, in his moral accounting, an asset on the balance sheet — a reduction of principal. This is pathological but coherent.

---

## VIII. POST-RESTORATION OPERATOR PHASE — c. 2012–2016

**Affect regulation.** The constricted-functional baseline of the mantle period without the scaffolding of the role. Insomnia entrenches; nightmares specific to Winter Soldier kills are depicted across the Brubaker solo, the Kot run, and the Rosenberg material. The absence of self-medication via alcohol or opioids across this period is, as noted in the prior assessment, diagnostic — it indicates that the suffering is being held *deliberately* as part of the atonement structure. He does not numb because numbing would be theft from the debt.

**Cognitive style.** Future-discounted to the mission horizon. He plans operations in detail; he does not plan a life. Asked where he will be in a year, he has no answer and the question registers as faintly insulting — a year is not a unit of time he is using.

**Self-concept.** Slow first-person integration. The "Winter Soldier" third-person reference attenuates across this period; by the late 2010s material he is using "I" for the Department X kills, which is — in Bromberg's "standing in the spaces" terms — the operationalization of integration: the capacity to hold the perpetrator-self and the present-self in a single experiential field without either collapsing.

**Attachment.** The Romanova partnership functions as the laboratory in which adult intimacy is, for the first time, sustained without handler-amputation. Its conspicuously non-domestic structure (safehouses, not homes; operators, not partners) is *protective accommodation* — both parties are working at the edge of their tolerance and have built a relational form that respects the edge. When her memory is altered and she forgets him, his acceptance is again concordance with loss: he has been trained, at the deepest level, that *bonds get taken*, and when one is taken he does not protest, because protest would imply he was owed it.

---

## IX. COSMIC / MAN-ON-THE-WALL PHASE — c. 2014–2018

**Affect regulation.** A new stability achieved through a precisely matched role. The Man-on-the-Wall function — preemptive lethal removal of cosmic threats so that more morally legible figures do not have to — is the rarest of clinical outcomes: an *exact fit* between pathological need (to carry unforgivable acts) and adaptive function (carrying acts that genuinely need to be carried). This is sublimation operating at peak efficiency. It is also, in a sense, a trap — the role rewards the very self-concept that ought to be loosening, and locks in the atonement economy as a *career.*

**Cognitive style.** Long-horizon strategic emerges for the first time since 1945, but only in the operational domain. He can plan a multi-year campaign against a threat class; he still cannot plan a Tuesday.

**Self-concept.** *The one who carries.* This is a more dignified packaging of the debtor-identity, but the underlying structure is unchanged.

**Attachment.** Sustained small in-group: Rogers, Romanova, Fury. Cosmic-isolation periods are tolerated without decompensation, which is itself a sign of internal-object stability — he can hold his people inside his head when they are not present.

---

## X. WHITE WOLF / WAKANDAN PHASE AND ITS AFTERMATH

**Affect regulation.** The Wakandan rehabilitation period — clean trigger-deconditioning, vibranium-prosthesis integration, structured agrarian routine, externally guaranteed safety — produces the first observable broadening of affective range since 1945. Positive affect is no longer reflexively suppressed; it is *permitted in small amounts, in supervised contexts.* The shift is incremental and is repeatedly destabilized by re-traumatization events, but the substrate change is real: he learns that he can feel something good without immediately being punished or punishing himself, and this learning, once installed, is not fully lost in subsequent decompensations.

**Cognitive style.** Reflective capacity expands. For the first time he can be asked *what do you want* and produce a non-mission answer — even if the answer is "I don't know yet."

**Self-concept.** The White Wolf identity is psychologically significant because it is *given to him by people who know what he did and chose to forgive him anyway.* This is the first identity in his life he has neither earned through service (the Army), been conditioned into (Department X), nor inherited from a dead man (Captain America). It is a gift, and his capacity to accept it is the single best prognostic indicator in the file.

**Attachment.** Expansion of the in-group to include Shuri and T'Challa — and crucially, these are bonds initiated *during* his damaged period, by people who never knew the pre-1945 self. They love the man who exists now. This is corrective relational experience at exactly the dose he can tolerate.

---

## XI. CURRENT PERIOD — RECENT THUNDERBOLTS / SOLO MATERIAL

**Affect regulation.** Stable constricted-functional with intermittent broadening. He can be in a room with people celebrating without leaving, though he will stand near the door. He can be thanked without flinching visibly, though the flinch is happening internally and a trained observer can see it. He can mentor (the Yelena material) — which requires tolerating being looked up to, a posture he resisted for decades.

**Cognitive style.** Integrated tactical-reflective. Plans missions; tentatively plans seasons. Will not yet plan years.

**Self-concept.** *Recovering, never recovered.* The integration is sufficient that he no longer needs splitting; the atonement economy is sufficiently entrenched that he does not believe in completion. This is, clinically, a livable outcome. It is not health in the textbook sense — the Griffin moral-injury triad's shame and self-condemnation poles remain elevated, and full remission is not on the table — but it is *function*, *connection*, and *meaning*, which is the three-legged stool the trauma-recovery literature considers the realistic ceiling for cases of this severity.

**Attachment.** Earned-secure with disorganized substrate, as the prior assessment correctly identifies. The substrate flares under intimacy-consolidation pressure (offers of domesticity, retirement, public honor); the earned-secure surface holds under everything else.

---

## XII. TRAJECTORY AND PROGNOSTIC SUMMARY

The decade-by-decade arc traces a near-canonical sequence: *integrated pre-trauma self → adaptive operational compartmentalization → catastrophic dismemberment of self → iatrogenic structural dissociation → forensic reconstruction → role-scaffolded re-stabilization → punishment-phase concordance → operator-phase consolidation → sublimation-phase career fit → corrective-relational broadening → integrated but permanently-marked current state.*

The prognosis is what the literature calls *partial sustained remission with vulnerability.* The vulnerabilities are stable and known to him: trigger-cue exposure, cold restraint, Russian-language interrogation morphology, threats to the small in-group, offers of normalcy. The strengths are also stable: the Rogers bond that predates the breakage and was never reached by it; the sublimatory channel; the small in-group that loves him in present tense; the procedural mastery; and — most importantly — the slow accumulation, across the post-Wakanda decade, of evidence in his own nervous system that *feeling good is not the same as betraying the dead.*

He will not arrive at the destination the recovery literature calls integration-and-meaning-making in its complete form. He will live, instead, in the long approach to it, which for a subject of this etiology and load is the actual best-case outcome and should be read as such.

— END SECTION —


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: BARNES, J. B.

*Prepared as Section 4 of the standing dossier. All diagnostic reasoning is derived from the longitudinal behavioral record (1941–present) and cross-referenced to the clinical literature retrieved by the guide: Griffin et al. (2019) on moral injury and van Dijke, Hopman & Ford (2018) on the discriminant boundary between complex PTSD and borderline personality disorder. Analog DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 codes are given for cross-system continuity; the subject has, to our knowledge, never been formally assessed inside a credentialed civilian psychiatric system, so all formulations are observer-derived from canonical conduct.*

---

## 4.1 Framing the Diagnostic Problem

The subject presents a near-unique forensic-psychiatric profile in the following respect: the etiologic events span more than seven decades of subjective time, encompass repeated coerced perpetration of homicide, were imposed via industrial-grade neuropsychiatric conditioning (sensory deprivation, ECT-analog memory suppression, pharmacological dissociatives, verbal-cue state induction, recursive cryogenic interruption of consolidation), and were terminated not by therapeutic intervention but by a single restorative event of extra-clinical character (the Cosmic Cube intervention, *Captain America* vol. 5 #14, 2006). There is no civilian analog to the index trauma. There is, however, a clinically tractable analog to its sequelae.

The conventional risk in cases of this profile is over-diagnosis — the temptation to load the chart with every overlapping condition the behavior superficially suggests (BPD, DID, psychotic-spectrum, ASPD, intermittent explosive). The opposite error, equally common, is reduction to a single label ("he has PTSD") that flattens a multi-axial presentation. Both errors are avoided here by working from the behavioral record outward to the smallest diagnostic set that exhaustively accounts for it.

The smallest such set, in our judgment, is **three** primary/co-primary conditions plus **two** secondary features, with a robust differential clearing six commonly mis-assigned alternatives.

---

## 4.2 Primary Diagnosis — Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder

**ICD-11: 6B41 (Complex PTSD).** **DSM-5-TR analog:** PTSD (309.81 / F43.10) with prominent dissociative symptoms, supplemented by features of Disorders of Extreme Stress Not Otherwise Specified (DESNOS, the proposed but unadopted DSM antecedent of CPTSD).

### 4.2.1 Etiologic Reconstruction

CPTSD per ICD-11 and the van Dijke et al. (2018) discriminant model requires (a) exposure to prolonged or repeated traumatic events from which escape was difficult or impossible, and (b) the three CPTSD-specific Disturbances in Self-Organization (DSO) clusters — affect dysregulation, negative self-concept, and disturbances in relationships — additional to the core PTSD triad of re-experiencing, avoidance, and persistent sense of current threat.

The subject's etiologic profile is layered:

- **Predisposing (childhood, c. 1925–1937):** loss of father (George Barnes, Camp Lehigh weapons-training accident); maternal absence in published record; institutional rearing on an active military installation; absorption of the moral and aesthetic codes of the U.S. Army before adolescence. This is not in itself traumatic in the Criterion A sense, but it produces the substrate van Dijke identifies as a CPTSD risk factor: early relational disruption combined with environmental valorization of obedience to authority and instrumentalized violence.
- **Priming (late 1930s–1941):** covert recruitment as a pre-Pearl Harbor wet-work asset by Army intelligence, per the Brubaker retcon (*Captain America* vol. 5, 2005 onward). The subject killed under government direction before he was legally an adult by modern standards. This installs the operational template — *I am the one who does what cannot be acknowledged* — that the Soviet program would later weaponize.
- **Criterion A index event (March 1945):** the Zemo drone explosion off Newfoundland. Catastrophic blast trauma, traumatic amputation of the left upper extremity, presumed concussive TBI, hypothermic immersion, presumed death of the primary attachment figure (Rogers). Any one of these would be sufficient for PTSD-criterion exposure. They occurred conjointly, in the absence of rescue by his own forces.
- **Prolonged interpersonal traumatization (c. 1945 – c. 1990s, with intermittent cryo-interruption):** Department X conditioning, repeated mind-wipes, coerced perpetration of homicide on at least three continents, induced romantic/relational attachments subsequently amputated by handler intervention (the Romanova relationship, *Winter Soldier* #1–5, 2012). This is the inescapable, prolonged, interpersonal trauma that defines the CPTSD etiologic profile per van Dijke et al. The element of *induced perpetration* further qualifies it for the moral-injury overlay treated separately in §4.3.
- **Re-traumatization (post-restoration, 2006–present):** Siberian extradition and gulag torture (*Captain America* #616 ff., 2011); repeated combat exposure under Avengers/Thunderbolts/Man-on-the-Wall operational roles; cyclic re-emergence of conditioning triggers under operational stress.

### 4.2.2 Symptom Presentation Mapped to the Behavioral Record

**Core PTSD cluster:**

- *Intrusion (DSM Criterion B / ICD re-experiencing):* canonical depiction of nightmares specific to Winter Soldier-era kills (Brubaker, Kot, Rosenberg runs); intrusive imagery cued by museum exhibits, archival photographs of his Winter Soldier deployments, and Russian-language environmental stimuli. He is shown, repeatedly, to startle minimally and silently — the intrusion is internal and visible only as a momentary tightening of the jaw or a held breath.
- *Avoidance (Criterion C / ICD avoidance):* refusal to attend public commemorations involving the 107th Infantry or his Winter Soldier-era victims' surviving relatives; geographic avoidance of specific safehouses and operational sites (Wakanda, Romania, and remote North American locations preferred over urban European theaters where deployments occurred); avoidance of mirrors, photography, and biographical interview.
- *Persistent sense of current threat (ICD) / Hyperarousal (DSM Criterion E):* chronic insomnia documented across at least four writers; nocturnal pacing routines; perimeter-checking behavior in safehouses; weapon-within-reach sleeping arrangements; tactical scanning on entering any room — the behavior described in §5 as "hypervigilant calm" is the *baseline*, not a stress state.

**CPTSD-specific DSO clusters (the discriminant features per van Dijke):**

- *Affect dysregulation, predominantly under-modulating type:* the subject's dysregulation manifests as constriction and shutdown rather than the over-modulating lability of BPD. Positive affect is more suppressed than negative. He tolerates grief, shame, and rage with operational composure; he cannot tolerate praise, celebration, or expressions of gratitude without acute discomfort and exit behavior. Dissociative episodes — partial state-switching under cue exposure — fall under this cluster per ICD-11.
- *Negative self-concept:* pervasive, stable, treatment-resistant. Operates from the organizing self-statement *I am the weapon that was used on people who didn't deserve it.* Evidence: gulag submission with equanimity (*Cap* #616 ff.); explicit instruction to Rogers not to extract him; voluntary acceptance of every available penance role (Man on the Wall, Thunderbolts black-ops, the most lethal mission profile in any team allocation); refusal of the Captain America mantle until guilt-leveraged by reference to Rogers's wishes.
- *Disturbances in relationships:* capacity for intimacy *is preserved* — this is diagnostically important. The disturbance is in *form*, not in *capacity*. He maintains stably valenced bonds (no idealization-devaluation cycling, no abandonment frenzy, no chronic emptiness) but structures them defensively: non-domestic, geographically dispersed, operationally framed. The Romanova partnership is the paradigm — intimate without cohabitation, partnered without marriage, mutually loyal without daily entanglement.

### 4.2.3 Course and Trajectory

Onset of full CPTSD presentation: dated to the restoration event of 2006, at which point the symptom set became subjectively accessible to the subject. (Prior to restoration, the subject was not phenomenally continuous with himself; symptoms in the Winter Soldier period were observable to others but not introspectively reportable.) Course since 2006 is best described as **chronic with partial, asymmetric remission**:

- Dissociative-state vulnerability has decreased substantially. Splitting in language ("the Winter Soldier" in third person, 2006–c. 2012) has integrated to first-person ownership of the period.
- Negative self-concept has *not* meaningfully remitted. It is structurally load-bearing — it organizes his pro-social conduct — and he resists interventions that target it directly. (See §4.6 on prognosis.)
- Avoidance and hyperarousal symptoms are stable. Sleep disturbance is unremitted.
- Relational capacity has expanded modestly (Wilson, Yelena, Shuri added to the trusted in-group since 2014).

---

## 4.3 Co-Primary Diagnosis — Moral Injury Syndrome

**Not yet a formal DSM/ICD entity; operationalized per Griffin et al. (2019), *Journal of Traumatic Stress* 32(3):350–362.** Distinguished from PTSD by etiology (transgression of moral schema rather than life-threat exposure) and phenomenology (shame, self-condemnation, spiritual/existential disorientation, social withdrawal, rather than fear-based hyperarousal). The two conditions frequently co-occur and produce additively impairing functional outcomes; treatment targets differ.

### 4.3.1 Why This Is a Paradigmatic Case

The Griffin et al. review makes the diagnostically critical point that **moral injury arises from acts that violate the subject's moral schema even when those acts were not freely chosen** — coercion, command authority, and impaired agency do not protect against the syndrome. They predict, on the basis of pooled data, the characteristic triad of *shame, self-condemnation, and social withdrawal,* with associated self-injurious sequelae.

The subject meets every element of this triad with a specificity that approaches textbook illustration:

- **Shame** (distinct from guilt — guilt is *I did a bad thing*; shame is *I am a bad thing*): the subject's organizing self-narrative is shame-coded. He does not say *I committed acts I regret*; he behaves as though he *is* the acts. Observable in body-language patterns at any public recognition event — head dipped, eyes off-axis, physical retreat toward the room's perimeter or exit.
- **Self-condemnation:** active rather than passive. He does not merely accept others' condemnation; he generates his own continuously. The Siberian extradition acceptance is the load-bearing example — given the choice between justice systems that would have plausibly absolved him on grounds of coercion (U.S., Wakandan) and the one most likely to convict and brutalize him (Russian), he selected the latter and instructed his allies not to interfere.
- **Social withdrawal:** structural, not episodic. The non-domestic relational architecture noted above; the recurrent self-removal after periods of intimacy; the preference for operational over social contexts; the choice, immediately after restoration, of supervised solitude (Fury) over reunion (Rogers).

### 4.3.2 Self-Injurious Sequelae

The Griffin review predicts elevated risk of self-injurious behavior in moral-injury cases. In this subject the prediction is borne out in a sublimated, mission-channeled form rather than as overt parasuicidal conduct: **recurrent voluntary uptake of assignments with expected non-return.** The Man-on-the-Wall role is the clearest case — a role whose constitutive function is to be the person who absorbs the unforgivable so others need not. He sought it. He has refused to step down from it when offered relief. He volunteers for the most lethal slot in any tactical allocation. This is *equivalent* to the predicted self-injurious sequela; it is laundered through operational utility, which is precisely what makes it durable and untreatable through conventional means.

### 4.3.3 Spiritual / Existential Dimension

Griffin et al. note an existential dimension that the PTSD construct does not capture — loss of meaning, loss of trust in moral order, alienation from previously held frameworks. The subject's specific manifestation is the **rejection of redemption as a terminal state**: he does not believe one *arrives* at being forgiven; he believes one *conducts oneself* in a particular way continuously. This is theologically literate and clinically diagnostic: it converts moral injury into a permanent vocational structure, which is functionally adaptive (sustains pro-social action) and clinically pathological (forecloses recovery).

---

## 4.4 Secondary Diagnosis — Other Specified Dissociative Disorder

**DSM-5-TR: 300.15 / F44.89.** **ICD-11: 6B6Y.** Operationally: residual dissociative-state vulnerability from imposed handler-conditioning, with substantial but incomplete integration post-restoration.

### 4.4.1 Why OSDD and Not DID

Dissociative Identity Disorder requires two or more distinct personality states with continuity, autobiographical specificity, and (typically) developmentally rooted etiology — most commonly originating in pre-pubertal severe trauma producing genuinely segregated identity organizations. The subject does not meet this profile. The "Winter Soldier" was not an organically developed alter; it was a **handler-induced operational state** built atop suppressed autobiographical memory via external conditioning. Critically, the Winter Soldier-state did not possess the autobiographical specificity of an alter — it possessed *operational competence and conditioned compliance* but referred to its own history only as fragmentary mission record.

Post-restoration evidence supports OSDD rather than DID:

- Initial third-person reference to the Winter Soldier period (splitting, dissociative distancing) has integrated to first-person reference across the 2010s.
- The subject experiences trigger-cue vulnerability (Russian phrase-strings, sensory cues of restraint, cold, electrode contact) as *intrusion upon his integrated self,* not as switching between equipotent identities.
- He has developed inhibitory countermeasures (described in canon as cognitive grounding routines, narrative self-statement, deliberate breath control) which presuppose a continuous executive self.

### 4.4.2 Residual Symptom Profile

- Trigger-cued partial state-switch under high-stress exposure; risk diminished but not eliminated.
- Conditioned somatic responses (freeze on restraint, autonomic reactivity to Russian-language interrogation register) persist below the threshold of full state-switch.
- Mild ongoing depersonalization in the moments immediately following trigger exposure — the subject describes (in canon, in dialogue with Romanova and Wilson) a sensation of "watching himself from outside" before reasserting executive control.

---

## 4.5 Secondary Diagnosis — Persistent Depressive Disorder, with Anxious Distress

**DSM-5-TR: 300.4 / F34.1.** **ICD-11: 6A72.** Specified rather than left to the CPTSD umbrella because the depressive features are independent of, and outlast, episodes of acute trauma reactivation.

Symptom presentation:

- *Chronic dysphoric mood* exceeding two years (in fact, nearly two decades since restoration); not better accounted for by a single major depressive episode.
- *Anhedonia* of a specific pattern — *positive-affect anhedonia* dominates; he experiences negative affects with full intensity. This asymmetry is itself diagnostic of survivor-guilt logic: pleasure is treated as a defection.
- *Sleep disturbance* (insomnia, nightmare-driven early awakening).
- *Persistent low self-worth* — overlapping with CPTSD negative self-concept but extending into anticipatory pessimism about future states.
- *Anxious distress features*: motor tension (perimeter-checking, hand-positioning vigilance over the prosthetic), inability to relax, anticipatory dread, fear that something awful will happen — operationalized as the chronic background expectation that his Winter Soldier-state may re-emerge.

This presentation is *not* better accounted for by a single MDD episode (course is chronic, not episodic), nor by bipolar-spectrum process (no hypomanic or manic history), nor by adjustment disorder (etiology is not a single discrete stressor and chronicity exceeds adjustment criteria).

---

## 4.6 Comorbidity Structure & Functional Interaction

The four diagnoses above are not independent. They form an interlocking structure:

- CPTSD provides the **substrate** (affect dysregulation, hyperarousal, negative self-concept, relational disturbance) on which the other conditions sit.
- Moral injury provides the **organizing narrative** — it converts the negative self-concept of CPTSD from a disorganized symptom into a coherent identity, which paradoxically stabilizes functioning while foreclosing recovery.
- OSDD provides the **acute vulnerability** — the residual mechanism by which novel stressors can produce partial decompensation.
- Persistent depressive disorder provides the **chronic affective floor** — the steady-state dysphoria that persists between acute episodes.

The functional consequence is a presentation that is **highly stable, highly impaired, and highly productive simultaneously.** The subject does not decompensate readily because his pathology is structured into a vocational identity. The same fact makes him resistant to standard trauma-focused therapy (he experiences symptomatic improvement as moral abdication) and unusually responsive to relational and meaning-based interventions (Wakandan rehabilitative framing under T'Challa/Shuri; sustained Rogers/Romanova/Wilson scaffolding).

Prognosis: **chronic, partially compensated, unlikely to remit to subclinical levels under any presently available intervention.** Expected course is continued high-functioning impairment with episodic acute exacerbations triggered by (a) novel exposure to surviving victims' families, (b) trigger-cue exposure under coercion, (c) loss or threat to in-group members. Risk of completed suicide is *paradoxically low* despite high suicidal-equivalent behavior (mission-channeled self-endangerment), because the atonement schema requires continued action; he cannot atone if he is dead. Risk of mission-incurred death is *elevated* and is the most probable mode of subject loss.

---

## 4.7 Rigorous Differential — What He Is NOT, and Why

The following conditions are *commonly mis-assigned* in cases of this profile and are explicitly excluded.

### 4.7.1 Borderline Personality Disorder (DSM 301.83 / ICD 6D10.5)

**Superficial overlap:** identity disturbance, intense relationships, self-damaging behavior, affective instability.

**Excluded on discriminant criteria per van Dijke, Hopman & Ford (2018):**

- *Abandonment dynamics:* BPD is defined by frantic efforts to avoid real or imagined abandonment. The subject's pattern is the opposite — he is the one who withdraws at points of bonding consolidation; he tolerates the loss of relationships (Romanova's memory alteration, accepted without protest) with a composure inconsistent with BPD organization.
- *Idealization–devaluation cycling:* absent. His attachments are stably valenced over decades — Rogers has never been devalued, even during periods of conflict; Romanova has never been idealized into a fantasy object.
- *Impulsive self-damaging behavior across multiple domains:* absent. His self-endangerment is exclusively mission-channeled and prosocial. He does not exhibit BPD-typical impulsive spending, substance use, binge eating, reckless sex, or reckless driving. The *channel* is restrictive in a way BPD impulsivity is not.
- *Chronic emptiness:* not present. The subject experiences chronic *guilt*, which is phenomenologically distinct from BPD emptiness — guilt has an object and a content; emptiness does not.
- *Identity disturbance:* present but **iatrogenic and historical**, not developmentally structural. BPD identity disturbance is a developmental failure of self-coherence; the subject's identity disturbance was *imposed externally* upon a previously coherent self that has substantially reasserted itself post-restoration.
- *Affective instability:* the BPD pattern is rapid lability across the affective spectrum, often hours-long. The subject's affective pattern is constriction with rare breakthrough, on timescales of weeks or months.

The van Dijke et al. discriminant analysis explicitly identifies the constellation the subject presents — chronic negative self-concept *without* abandonment frenzy, *without* idealization-devaluation, *without* multi-domain impulsivity — as belonging on the CPTSD side of the boundary, not the BPD side.

### 4.7.2 Dissociative Identity Disorder (DSM 300.14 / ICD 6B64)

**Excluded** as detailed in §4.4.1: the Winter Soldier was an imposed handler-state, not a developmentally rooted alter, lacked autobiographical specificity as an identity, and integrated to first-person ownership rather than persisting as a parallel personality structure. The residual presentation is properly OSDD.

### 4.7.3 Antisocial Personality Disorder (DSM 301.7 / ICD 6D10.2)

**Superficial overlap:** extensive history of homicide, capacity for instrumental violence, comfort with deception in operational contexts.

**Excluded** on every discriminant criterion:

- ASPD requires conduct disorder before age 15. No evidence; the early-life record shows precisely the opposite — institutional good conduct, attachment-seeking, pro-social orientation.
- ASPD requires pervasive disregard for the rights of others. The subject's entire post-restoration architecture is built on hypervigilant *regard* for the rights of others, to the point of pathological over-correction.
- ASPD is characterized by *absence* of remorse. The subject presents with hypertrophied remorse — moral injury is the inverse of antisocial conduct.
- ASPD impulsivity, irritability, aggressiveness, and irresponsibility are absent or inverted. The subject is the model of disciplined responsibility within his chosen vocation.

The Winter Soldier-era homicides are correctly understood as **coerced state-actions under conditions that vitiate moral agency**, not as expressions of antisocial character. The pre-restoration period therefore does not even meet the


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: BARNES, J. B.

*Catalog compiled from longitudinal observation across the published record (1941–present); cross-referenced to clinical sources (Griffin 2019; van Dijke 2018). Organized by state. Granularity to the level of micro-tells: posture, gaze, hand, breath, language, route. Where canon is silent, inference is marked as such and grounded in the established pattern.*

---

## I. BASELINE — THE "CALM" STATE

There is no true calm. What presents as calm is **regulated vigilance** — the operator at rest who has never actually left the operating theater. Catalog this state carefully because every other state is a deviation from it.

**Posture and station-keeping.** Sits with his back to a wall by default; if no wall is available, he angles the chair forty-five degrees off the room's center of mass so both the primary entrance and the largest blind seam are inside a single saccade. Will rearrange chairs in a room he is entering before sitting — a small, unannounced shuffle disguised as restlessness. Does not lean. The torso is held a fraction forward of vertical, weight slightly on the balls of the feet even when seated, which means he can stand without using his hands. Across multiple writers he is shown standing first when anyone enters; this is not courtesy.

**The left arm at rest.** Hangs loose at his side or rests palm-down on the thigh, never crossed over the right. The metal hand is kept out of casual contact with other people's bodies — he does not clap shoulders with it, does not shake hands with it, does not gesture with it in conversation. When he does gesture, it is the right hand exclusively. The left is treated as ordnance, not appendage.

**Gaze.** Tracks in a slow horizontal sweep approximately every eleven to fifteen seconds when nominally inattentive — the rhythm of a posted sentry, not of casual looking. Eye contact with trusted others is sustained and direct; with strangers, brief and re-checking. He looks at hands before faces in any new encounter — a habit canonically depicted from the *Winter Soldier* solo runs onward, and a tell of someone whose threat-assessment template was built around concealed weapons.

**Breath.** Diaphragmatic, slow, four-count in and six-count out under normal conditions — a regulated cadence consistent with trained breath-control rather than relaxed autonomic state. Under stress the count compresses; he does not lose the cadence, only tightens it.

**Verbal baseline.** Economy bordering on miserliness. Sentences average shorter than his pre-war record (the 1940s Barnes was voluble; the present Barnes is not). Dry register. Sardonic humor when comfortable, almost always at his own expense. He does not initiate small talk; he tolerates it from Rogers, Wilson, and Yelena with visible affection; he will close it on anyone else inside three exchanges.

**Decision-making at rest.** Plans missions in granular five-stage sequences; plans his own life in horizons of seventy-two hours. Asked where he will be in a year, he produces no answer. This is not evasion. He genuinely does not project that far on his own behalf.

---

## II. UNDER MILD STRESS — DISRUPTION OF ROUTINE, MINOR UNCERTAINTY

The first observable deviation from baseline is **the loss of the joke**. Humor is the load-bearing tell of his comfort; when it goes, registration begins.

- **Verbal economy tightens.** Sentences become declaratives; questions vanish.
- **Hand inventory.** The right hand will move once to confirm the presence of a concealed knife — typically a small fixed blade carried at the small of the back or inside the left boot, depending on era. The check is a single pass disguised as adjusting a belt or pant leg.
- **Re-anchoring of the left arm.** The metal hand will close into a loose fist and reopen once, slowly. This is not a tell he is aware of. Across Brubaker's run and into Kot/Rosenberg material it is depicted as a near-involuntary calibration gesture — confirmation that the prosthesis responds, confirmation that he is in his body.
- **Geographic micro-adjustment.** He will move three to five feet, no more, to bring a second exit into his line of sight. He will do this while ostensibly fetching coffee or examining a wall.
- **Withdrawal of physical proximity from non-combatants.** He steps back from civilians under mild stress, not toward them. The protective instinct is to *clear his own footprint* from their vicinity, not close on them.

---

## III. UNDER MODERATE STRESS — ACTIVE OPERATIONAL CONDITIONS

He takes over. This is the most reliable behavioral signature in the canon: under moderate operational stress, regardless of nominal command structure, Barnes assumes tactical lead. He does it without announcing it and frequently without being noticed doing it.

- **Speech becomes imperative.** Two- to five-word commands. "Left side." "On me." "Down." "Wait." Question-form disappears entirely.
- **Movement.** Center of gravity drops; gait shortens; he moves on the outside edges of his feet, which silences impact. He covers ground in arcs rather than straight lines, using cover even where no shooter is present — a habit so ingrained it functions in unthreatened spaces.
- **Weapons handling.** Long gun shouldered low-ready, never high-ready (high-ready obscures peripheral vision and reads as untrained on him); handgun retention-grip when transitioning through doors. He reloads before empty, not at empty — a discipline of someone whose conditioning will not permit a click in a fight.
- **Use of the prosthesis.** Becomes weapon-forward. He will block edged weapons with the left arm, present the left shoulder to incoming fire, and use the left hand for the kills he does not want the right hand to remember making. This is observable across multiple writers and is psychologically legible: *the arm given to him by his torturers does the killing; the arm he was born with does not.* Even after the Wakandan replacement, the lateralization persists. The body remembers the division of labor.
- **Eye contact with allies.** Drops. He stops looking at the people he is working with and tracks only threats and angles. Information transfer becomes hand-signal or single-word call.

---

## IV. UNDER HIGH STRESS — LETHAL DEPLOYMENT

The state his conditioning was designed to produce, now operating in service of choices he has made.

- **Affect goes flat.** Witnesses across canon describe the face as "blank," "empty," "doll-like." This is not dissociation in the clinical sense; it is volitional affective shutdown, a learned suppression of the facial musculature that would otherwise leak intent.
- **Breath cadence compresses to four-count both directions and locks there.** Audible only at extreme proximity.
- **Speech ceases almost entirely.** He will issue one-word commands and otherwise operate in silence. He does not shout. He does not announce contact. Allies who have not worked with him repeatedly find this unnerving; allies who have, do not.
- **Kinetics.** Movement becomes economical to the point of appearing slow. He does not lunge. He arrives. The kill is concluded before observers register the initiation. The published record consistently depicts this — opponents are dispatched mid-sentence, mid-step, in the white space between panels.
- **Pain processing offline.** He continues operating through injuries that should drop him. Inferred sequela of cryogenic and torture conditioning: nociception is present but not behaviorally gating.
- **Post-engagement shutdown.** Inside ninety seconds of action ending, the activation collapses. He sits, often on the floor, often with his back against the nearest vertical surface, and goes quiet for two to five minutes. Does not want to be touched in this window. Will tolerate Rogers's hand on his shoulder; will tolerate Romanova sitting beside him in silence; will not tolerate anyone else's intervention. Comes back online by a small physical re-anchoring — a slow flex of the left hand, a knuckle pressed once to the right eye, a breath audibly released.

---

## V. TRIGGER-CUE EXPOSURE — RESIDUAL CONDITIONING

Distinct from stress response. The conditioning substrate persists and can be activated by specific stimuli regardless of operational state.

**Cue inventory** (compiled from canon):
- Russian phrase-strings of the Department X protocol class.
- Restraint at the wrists, particularly metal-on-metal.
- Cold below approximately 4°C combined with confinement.
- Electrode contact at the temples or base of the skull.
- A specific tonal register of command-Russian delivered without affect.
- Inferred: the smell of certain industrial solvents associated with the maintenance bay (this is inference from his documented avoidance of mechanic environments, not stated in canon).

**Response under cue, partial:** pupillary dilation; a hard single inhale; the left hand opening fully and then closing; a momentary saccade-loss where his eyes lock forward. He recovers from partial cues in seconds and visibly so — a head-shake, a swallow, a return of gaze. He will not discuss the cue afterward unless directly asked by Rogers or Romanova.

**Response under cue, full:** state-switch with diminished volitional inhibition. Decreasing across the published timeline as integration consolidates. He has developed counter-conditioning protocols (named in the Brubaker material as deliberate self-work with Fury and later with Wakandan handlers); these are partially effective. The substrate has not been eliminated and on the evidence cannot be.

---

## VI. INTIMACY — THE STATE HE TRUSTS LEAST

Defined here as the condition of being known by another person without operational pretext. He is more comfortable under fire than in this state and the behavioral record shows it.

- **Physical proximity.** With Rogers: stands close, often within arm's reach, frequently shoulder-to-shoulder rather than face-to-face — the side-by-side configuration of two soldiers, not the face-to-face of two civilians. With Romanova: closer still, but the contact is functional — a hand at the back, a knee touching a knee, never the extended postures of public couples. With Wilson and Yelena: warmer than he allows himself to admit; will accept a clap on the shoulder from Wilson that he would deflect from any other man.
- **Eye contact in intimacy.** Sustained but intermittent. He looks away at the moments most people look toward — when something tender has just been said, when affection has been received. The look-away is not avoidance of the other person; it is avoidance of being seen receiving the thing.
- **Verbal disclosure.** Slow, oblique, often retroactive. He tells stories of the Winter Soldier years in fragments, in operational register, stripped of affect — the affect is left for the listener to supply. When the listener supplies it (Rogers's quiet, Romanova's silence, Wilson's "Jesus, Buck"), he absorbs the response without comment and the conversation moves on. The disclosure is the gift; the response is not requested.
- **Touch initiation.** Rare. When he initiates, it is with the right hand. A palm to the back of Rogers's neck. A thumb to Romanova's cheekbone. A hand at the small of Yelena's back guiding her out of a room. The left hand he keeps to himself in these moments — even with people who have explicitly told him they do not mind it.
- **The withdrawal pattern.** After episodes of consolidated intimacy — a long conversation, a shared night, a public acknowledgment of what they are to each other — he will geographically remove himself within twenty-four to seventy-two hours. Not a break, not an ending; a circuit-breaker. Goes on a mission. Goes to ground. Returns when the activation has discharged. The closest people in his life have learned to read this and not interpret it as rejection. The literature on disorganized attachment (Main; see also van Dijke's CPTSD relational-disturbance cluster) predicts exactly this oscillation.

---

## VII. GRIEF

He is competent at grief in a way that is itself diagnostic — a man with this much practice.

- **External register.** Quiet. He does not weep publicly except on extremely rare canonical occasions (Rogers's death; the Siberian sequence). When he does, the weeping is silent and brief and conducted with his face turned away.
- **Behavioral signature.** Increased work. He takes more missions, sleeps less, eats with even less interest than baseline. The grief is metabolized through action.
- **Ritual.** He visits graves alone, at off-hours, without flowers — the flowers feel performative to him. He stands. He does not speak aloud. Inferred: he inventories the dead in a private mental list and revisits it on calendar anchors (the anniversary of the 1945 fall; the anniversary of Rogers's assassination; the dates of specific Winter Soldier kills he has been able to identify).
- **Verbal handling.** Will not eulogize. Asked to speak at memorials he declines or speaks in fewer than fifty words. The brevity is not coldness; it is the refusal to perform an emotion he experiences as private property.
- **Containment failure mode.** When grief exceeds the bandwidth of his work-channel, the dissociative substrate is more vulnerable. The Siberian extradition occurs in such a window; the gulag submission is, read carefully, a man using imprisonment as a structural container for a grief he cannot otherwise hold.

---

## VIII. VICTORY — THE STATE HE FAILS AT MOST CONSISTENTLY

The most reliable diagnostic in the dossier. Watch him at any celebration in the canon. He is not there, or he is there for fewer than twenty minutes, or he is there at the wall, holding a drink he is not drinking, scanning exits.

- **Bodily signature of victory-discomfort.** Shoulders rise slightly (the opposite of relaxation); the left hand closes; the gaze drops more frequently than it raises; the verbal economy tightens rather than loosens. He smiles, briefly, when directly addressed; the smile does not reach the eyes and does not survive the speaker's looking away.
- **Avoidance of toast and acknowledgment.** Will deflect verbally ("Steve did the heavy lifting"; "Romanoff called the play") with reflexive consistency. Will physically leave the room if praise concentrates. This is exploitable, per the personality synthesis, and has been exploited by allies wanting him absent from photographs.
- **Post-victory action.** Goes to clean weapons. Goes to debrief. Goes to write the after-action. Finds the unfinished operational thread and pulls on it. The behavior is *not* survivor's guilt expressed as discomfort; it is the active refusal of the experiential reward, because the reward implies a closed account and his account is not closeable.

Compare Griffin et al. (2019) on moral injury: the literature specifies that moral-injury sufferers experience positive collective events as alienating, because the celebration narrative excludes their internal record of what was done. Barnes is a textbook case of this exclusion enacted in real time.

---

## IX. DEFEAT

Asymmetrically tolerated. He takes defeat better than victory. Defeat is congruent with his self-concept; victory is not.

- **Acceptance posture.** Goes still. Looks at the ground. Inventories what was lost in declarative sentences, often spoken aloud to a single other person in clipped after-action prose. Assigns himself the largest share of the failure regardless of actual causal weight.
- **Punishment-seeking.** Will volunteer for the recovery mission, the cleanup, the retrieval of bodies. Will take the watch no one else wants. This is the moral-injury sequela predicted by the literature — self-injurious behavior channeled through legitimized assignment.
- **Refusal of comfort, conditional.** Rejects pity. Accepts company. The distinction is sharp and consistent: he will sit with Rogers in silence for an hour after a failed operation; he will leave the room if Rogers offers absolution.
- **Recovery curve.** Faster than victory recovery. He is operational again within a sleep cycle. The defeat has been filed; the next operation is the response. He does not ruminate verbally. The rumination is internal and chronic and forms part of the baseline dysphoria the diagnostic record captures as persistent depressive features.

---

## X. SLEEP, NIGHT, AND THE SMALL HOURS

Behavioral record consistent across Brubaker, Kot, Remender, Rosenberg.

- **Sleep onset.** Difficult. Typically three to five hours per night, broken. Falls asleep most reliably when another trusted person is in the structure — not in the room, in the structure — a perimeter condition.
- **Position.** On the right side, left arm down. Inferred: the left arm down places the prosthesis between his body and any approach from the door side of the bed.
- **Nightmares.** Specific to identified Winter Soldier kills. Recurs across decades. He does not describe content; he describes the time he woke. The depiction across writers shows him sitting up without startling — a slow rise, a swing of the legs, a walk to the window. Does not return to bed until first light.
- **Nocturnal routes.** Paces. Inferred granular detail: walks the structure perimeter once on waking, checks sightlines, returns to a kitchen or common space, sits with coffee, waits. Reads when reading material is available — military history, Russian-language fiction (an intimate use of the language that conditioned him; a deliberate reclamation), occasional crime procedurals. Does not watch screens at night; the flicker disturbs his vigilance.
- **First contact in the morning.** Whoever finds him first finds a man who has been awake for hours and will not admit it. He will have already made coffee for them.

---

## XI. EATING, DRINKING, CONSUMPTION

- **Eating.** Functional. Eats what is in front of him without commentary. Preferences inferable rather than stated: tolerates Russian food without enthusiasm (the association is contaminated); eats American diner food with the closest thing to pleasure he displays at table — a 1940s anchor. Eats with the right hand; the left rests on his thigh, not the table.
- **Alcohol.** Drinks rarely and lightly. The canonical near-absence of intoxication is itself the diagnostic — a man with this trauma load who does not self-medicate is a man who has decided the relief is not earned. Will accept one drink at a gathering and nurse it. Will not be drunk in the presence of anyone he protects.
- **Caffeine.** Heavy. Coffee black, throughout the day and night.
- **Tobacco.** Smoked in the 1940s. Inferred: stopped during the Winter Soldier period (a habit handlers would not maintain for him); has not resumed. Will occasionally accept a cigarette in a stressful field context as a social gesture and not inhale.

---

## XII. SPEECH — REGISTER, LANGUAGE, LEXICAL TELLS

- **Native register.** 1940s Brooklyn cadence, attenuated by decades but resurfacing under fatigue and around Rogers. Specific lexical fossils: "pal," "swell" (rare, ironic), "fellas," the syllabic compression of "gonna/gotta/oughta" that the modern American mouth has largely lost. These markers intensify in proportion to the comfort of the company.
- **Operational register.** Stripped, precise, military-current. Switches register cleanly mid-conversation when the situation shifts; the switch is one of the cleanest behavioral signatures of his state.
- **Languages.** English (native, 1940s substrate). Russian (fluent, conditioned, contaminated — speaks it competently and with reluctance; uses it deliberately when reclamation is the point). German (functional, WWII-era). Inferred Romanian, Czech, Polish at survival level from Winter Soldier deployments. Wakandan acquired in basics during the White Wolf period; will use a phrase of greeting and otherwise defer to English.
- **Profanity.** Sparing, mid-register, era-anchored ("hell," "damn," the occasional harder word under acute stress). Does not curse around children. Does not blaspheme around Rogers, who he knows would not care but who he treats as if he might.
- **The third-person Winter Soldier.** Early post-restoration, he refers to "the Winter Soldier" in the third person — "he did that"; "the Soldier killed him." This usage decreases visibly across the 2010s canon. By the most recent material it is rare and used only with deliberate distancing intent. The integration is real; the substrate is not gone.

---

## XIII. DECISION HABITS — RULES OF THE INTERNAL OPERATING SYSTEM

Distilled across the record:

1. **Default to the harder option when assigning roles to himself, the easier option when assigning roles to others.** Volunteers for the breach, the rear guard, the long stalk, the kill no one wants on their record.
2. **Trust slowly; once given, trust completely.** Has perhaps six names on the interior list. The list does not churn.
3. **Distrust systems categorically.** Will execute lawful orders, will refuse unlawful ones, will not telegraph the distinction.
4. **Never lie to the interior list. Lie freely to everyone else when operational necessity requires.** Will undertake elaborate deception of strangers without compunction; will not deceive Rogers about an injury.
5. **Refuse leadership offered voluntarily; accept it when guilt-leveraged.** A consistent pattern that handlers and allies have learned to use. He cannot accept authority as a reward; he accepts it as a debt.
6. **Plan missions in detail. Plan life in days.** The future-discounting is structural and unlikely to change.
7. **Do not be photographed if avoidable.** Inferred from his absence in canonical group photographs and his documented avoidance of public events.
8. **Carry redundant blade.** A small fixed blade is on his person across nearly every depicted scene, including domestic ones. The canonical record is consistent enough on this that absence is significant.
9. **Always know the exit. Always know the second exit. Always know what is behind the wall.**
10. **When the choice is between his own life and an interior-list life, the choice is not a choice.** It has been pre-decided. The behavioral signature of this rule is the *absence* of the deliberative pause others would show in the moment — he moves without hesitation because there is nothing to deliberate.

---

## XIV. THE TELLS HE DOES NOT KNOW HE HAS

A surveillance file's most valuable section. Items he is not aware of, observable to a sustained observer.

- **The left-hand calibration flex** — a slow open-and-close of the prosthesis when his attention is occupied and his stress is rising. He does not register doing it. The frequency of the flex is the most reliable continuous metric of his internal state.
- **The right-thumb pass across the left forearm** — a single brushing motion across the seam where flesh would have met metal on the original Soviet prosthesis. Persists with the Wakandan arm despite the absence of the seam. A somatic memory of the boundary between *him* and *the weapon*. Occurs in moments of unguarded reflection.
