These are the levers of greatest tensile strength. Every adversary who has ever moved him at scale has moved him through one of these.

### I.a — Rogers

The master lever. Eighty years of canon converge on a single behavioral law: **a credible threat to, or invocation of, Steven Rogers reorganizes Barnes's entire decision stack within seconds.** Mission objectives are subordinated, self-preservation is suspended, time-horizon collapses to the immediate. The mechanism is older than the Winter Soldier conditioning; it predates the war. It is the original attachment, formed in adolescence to the first stable male figure available to a parentified orphan, and it has never been successfully displaced — not by Karpov, not by Lukin, not by the Cube, not by Rogers's own death, not by Rogers's eventual aging-out of the active mantle.

- **Protective handling.** Anyone briefing Barnes on a Rogers-involved situation must front-load *what Steve already knows and has already decided.* He tolerates Rogers being in danger if he has been informed that Rogers chose the danger with eyes open. The destabilizing form is *Rogers in jeopardy without Rogers's consent* — the "Steve doesn't know yet" framing collapses his judgment.
- **Calming use.** When dysregulated, the question "what would Steve want you to do in the next ten minutes" reliably re-anchors him. He uses Rogers as a superego proxy and will accept the proxy-voice from a trusted intermediary (Wilson, Romanova, Carter) when Rogers himself is unavailable.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** Faked Rogers distress signals; recordings; deepfaked voice; impersonation. He has been burned on this exact vector before and *still* runs toward it. The countermeasure is not skepticism — he cannot afford skepticism here — it is a pre-arranged duress code with Rogers that has been rotated since the 2010s.

### I.b — Romanova

Different valence, equal weight. The Romanova bond is the one relationship Barnes formed while *not himself*, that survived him becoming himself again. He treats it as evidence that something in him was real even during the unmaking — which means a threat to Natasha threatens not only her but the proof-of-self she constitutes for him.

- **Protective handling.** Their working pattern is non-domestic by design — safehouses, parallel ops, scheduled silences. Pressuring him toward a domestic configuration with her destabilizes both of them; allowing the operator-intimacy as it stands keeps him regulated.
- **Calming use.** Her presence shortens his post-action shutdown windows by an order of magnitude. She is the only person who can interrupt a dissociative narrowing without him reading the interruption as a threat.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** Memory-alteration of Natasha (which has occurred) is uniquely cruel to him — it reactivates the Department X template of "attachment is the punishment." He absorbs the loss with terrifying quietness and then accepts higher-lethality assignments for months.

### I.c — The Small Named In-Group

Wilson, Yelena, Shuri, T'Challa, Carter. The list is short and specific — generalized appeals to "your friends" or "your team" register weakly; named individuals register absolutely. Yelena holds a special sub-position: a younger operator from the same program, whose existence permits him to do for another what no one did for him. Threatening Yelena triggers a parental-protective response disproportionate to the length of their relationship.

- **Adversary use to anticipate.** Anyone with access to the in-group roster can move him via any of its members. The roster is small enough to defend.

### I.d — The Dead

Not living attachments but unfinished ones. The Winter Soldier kill list — particularly named victims, particularly the ones with surviving family — functions as a parallel attachment system. He cannot protect them retroactively, so he protects them prospectively through the proxy of their survivors. **Any survivor of a Winter Soldier–era victim who approaches him will be received, heard, and offered restitution in whatever form they name, up to and including his life.** This is exploitable. He knows it is exploitable. He has decided the exploitability is part of the debt.

---

## II. THE CONDITIONED SUBSTRATE (Iatrogenic Vulnerability Class)

Department X built leverage into his nervous system on purpose. Restoration has reduced but not eliminated the substrate. Treat the following as a *standing wound* that can be reopened by sufficiently precise stimuli.

### II.a — The Phrase-Strings

The Russian trigger-word protocols. Post-restoration he has developed inhibitory countermeasures — meditative pre-loading, somatic anchoring, a memorized counter-sequence of his own choosing — but the substrate is intact. Under sleep deprivation, hypothermia, restraint, or combined stressors, the inhibition thins.

- **Protective handling.** The exact phrase-string roster is canonically held by a vanishingly small number of people. Operational security on that roster is the single highest-value protective measure for him. Anyone who learns it should be considered as dangerous to him as a man with a knife at his throat.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** Partial triggers — fragments of the string, Russian-accented voices reading other content, the cadence without the words — produce sub-clinical activation: pupil dilation, micro-freeze, verbal economy collapse. He will not report these. Observers must.

### II.b — The Sensory Cue Set

Independent of language: **cold below approximately 4°C with concurrent restraint; electrode contact on the temples or sternum; the specific smell of cryostasis coolant (he describes it consistently across writers as "wet metal and ozone"); supine restraint on a reclined dental-style chair; the click-hiss of pneumatic actuators of the configuration used on the original arm.** Any of these in isolation produces discomfort; in combination, partial state-regression.

- **Protective handling.** Medical and dental procedures require pre-briefing and, where possible, modification of equipment posture (he tolerates seated procedures far better than supine). MRI is genuinely difficult for him and should be scheduled with an attending who knows the history.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** A sophisticated interrogator does not need the phrase-strings if they have the sensory set. He has been broken once by men who built a room for the purpose. He fears rooms.

### II.c — The Arm

The left upper extremity is somatically loaded as autobiography. The Wakandan vibranium prosthesis is a *gift from the forgiven*, which functions as ongoing reparative input — every time he uses it he is touching evidence that someone chose to repair him. Damage to the arm is therefore disproportionately destabilizing: it is not equipment loss, it is regression to the handler-dependency configuration.

- **Protective handling.** Maintenance access through Wakandan channels only. He will not accept arm service from anyone else and the refusal is correct — handler-dependency was deliberately engineered into the Soviet version and any non-Wakandan technician represents a vector for re-engineering it.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** EMP or vibranium-disruption weapons targeted at the arm aim not at his combat capacity but at his *sense of ownership of his own body.*

### II.d — Sleep

Chronic insomnia, nightmares specific to Winter Soldier kills, nocturnal pacing. Sleep deprivation is the master amplifier — every other vulnerability in this document intensifies in proportion to hours awake.

- **Protective handling.** Quiet, single-occupancy, weapons-accessible sleeping arrangements. He sleeps better when he can hear who is moving in the building. White-noise machines are counterproductive; they mask the data he uses to feel safe.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** Any operation against him should be expected to begin with a sleep-disruption phase. Forty-eight hours awake is roughly the threshold at which his inhibitory countermeasures against the phrase-strings begin to fail.

---

## III. THE MORAL ARCHITECTURE (Atonement Leverage Class)

The master motive. Any narrative framing that positions an action as installment-payment on the debt will receive serious consideration; any framing that positions an action as personal benefit will be reflexively refused.

### III.a — The "What Steve Would Want" Operator

He can be moved only by reference to the lost-and-returned attachment object's imputed will. Sharon Carter and Fury used this to make him take the shield. Rogers himself uses it sparingly because he knows it works absolutely. **It is the single most powerful persuasive lever available against his stated preferences.** Overuse will eventually corrode it; current canonical use is once or twice per arc, which preserves its weight.

- **Ethical caveat.** Using this lever to move him toward an action that *Steve would not actually want* is among the most damaging things that could be done to him, because it would teach him to mistrust the operator itself. Anyone with access to it has a fiduciary obligation not to lie.

### III.b — The Mission Nobody Else Will Take

The Man-on-the-Wall pattern. Offer him an assignment framed as (a) necessary, (b) morally compromising, (c) refused by all other qualified operators, and his refusal rate approaches zero. The framing satisfies all three drives simultaneously: atonement (he carries the unforgivable so others don't), protection (he removes a threat to the in-group), and containment (the weapon points the right way).

- **Protective handling.** The people around him have a standing obligation to *not* offer him these missions when alternatives exist. He will not refuse on his own behalf; the refusal must be made for him.
- **Adversary use to anticipate.** A false framing of a mission as a no-alternative no-volunteer assignment will draw him into theaters he should not enter. Verification protocols on mission-origin are protective.

### III.c — Survivor-Witness Encounters

A surviving family member of a named Winter Soldier kill, presented to him in a controlled setting, will receive whatever they ask for. This includes confessions, testimony, the offer of his life, and — most dangerously — the offer of *information* that he would otherwise hold operationally. A sufficiently coached false-survivor is a near-perfect intelligence extraction vector against him.

- **Protective handling.** Verification of survivor identity by a third party (Romanova has historically taken this role) before any unmediated contact. He will accept the verification step if it is framed as protection of the survivor, not protection of himself.

### III.d — The Refusal of Forgiveness

Counterintuitive but critical. **Telling him he is forgiven, recovered, past it, or done — destabilizes him.** The proposition denies the debt, which denies the organizing narrative, which leaves him without a structure. He responds to such statements with polite withdrawal followed by an uptick in self-handicapping behavior over the following weeks.

- **Protective handling.** The therapeutically correct register is *acknowledgment without dismissal*: "you were not the one who chose those acts, and you are still the one carrying them, and both are true." This is what Shuri and T'Challa got right in the White Wolf period. It is what well-meaning new acquaintances get wrong.

---

## IV. SOCIAL & CEREMONIAL VULNERABILITIES (Positive-Affect Aversion Class)

The constriction of positive affect is operationally exploitable.

### IV.a — Celebration

Award ceremonies, parades, public thanks, anniversaries, birthdays (his own — he has had over a hundred and does not acknowledge them), promotions, medals. Any of these produce acute discomfort and reliable avoidance behavior. **He will leave a room to escape applause.** Adversaries wishing to remove him from a venue can do so by arranging that he be celebrated in it.

- **Calming use.** When debriefing him after a successful operation, the correct register is *operational acknowledgment* ("the egress went clean, the asset is recovered"), not *personal praise* ("you did extraordinary work"). He metabolizes the former and chokes on the latter.

### IV.b — Public Identification

He tolerates being seen; he does not tolerate being *seen as significant.* Cameras, journalists, public-facing roles produce a withdrawal response. The White Wolf period in Wakanda worked partly because the Wakandan honorific was bestowed quietly within a community that did not televise its esteem.

### IV.c — Gifts

Material gifts produce immediate discomfort followed by displacement — he will give the gift away, repurpose it for operational use, or refuse it outright. The exceptions are *functional* gifts (a knife, a coat, the arm itself) which he accepts because they can be coded as tools rather than tributes.

### IV.d — Domesticity

The most destabilizing offer that can be made to him. A house, a partner who comes home, a routine that is not a mission. The instability is not because he cannot perform domesticity — he can, and the 1940s record shows he was warm and present in unstructured time — but because accepting it requires *believing he is allowed*, and that belief contradicts the atonement narrative at its root.

- **Protective handling.** Steps toward stability must be framed as operational requirements (a safehouse he must maintain; a base of operations; a cover identity that requires upkeep) rather than as life choices. Over time the framing can be softened, but premature softening triggers withdrawal.

---

## V. AUTHORITY & INSTITUTIONAL VULNERABILITIES

### V.a — Compliant-in-Form Pattern

He executes lawful orders, sabotages unlawful ones, and does not announce which is which. This means a corrupt institution will not know he has turned against them until after the fact. It also means a *misread* institution can lose him to a friction event he never warned them about. Operationally, anyone running him needs to understand that his compliance is conditional and silent.

### V.b — Aversion to Systems, Trust in Individuals

He will not trust an organization, ever. He will trust a person within an organization. This means the protective architecture around him must be built of *named handlers with persistent identity*, not rotating duty officers. A change of handler is, for him, a small re-traumatization, and the new handler must expect a months-long re-qualification period during which he will be courteous, watchful, and operationally honest but personally closed.

### V.c — Russian and Soviet-Successor State Contexts

Anything bearing the linguistic, aesthetic, or institutional markers of the Department X period activates conditioned wariness. He can operate in such contexts — has done so repeatedly — but the operating cost is elevated and the post-action shutdown is longer. Deploying him into Russophone theaters without acknowledgment of this cost is a form of carelessness that compounds over years.

---

## VI. PHYSIOLOGICAL & BODILY LEVERS

### VI.a — Restraint

Any form of restraint — handcuffs, straps, harnesses, even prolonged passenger-seat configurations on long transit — produces elevated arousal and, at sufficient duration, partial state-regression. He has learned to tolerate operational restraint (parachute harnesses, climbing rigs) by recoding it as task-equipment, but the recoding is effortful and breaks down under fatigue.

### VI.b — Cold

The cryostasis substrate. He runs warmer than he used to (deliberately overdresses, prefers heated environments, sleeps under more bedding than the ambient temperature warrants) and the preference is therapeutic, not stylistic. Cold-exposure interrogation is uniquely dangerous to him.

### VI.c — Medical Procedures

Anything involving the supine position, head restraint, IV access in the right arm (his only flesh arm above the elbow), or anesthesia must be conducted with full briefing and a trusted person physically present at induction and emergence. He will refuse procedures rather than undergo them without these conditions, and the refusal is correct — emergence from anesthesia is a known vulnerability window for state-regression.

### VI.d — Hunger and Thirst

He under-eats and under-hydrates under operational stress (somatic neglect noted in primary assessment). This compounds every cognitive and inhibitory vulnerability above. Anyone tracking his condition should monitor intake the way one would monitor a pilot's hours.

---

## VII. THE THINGS THAT WILL NOT WORK (Negative Leverage — Use as Adversary-Behavior Indicators)

The following are levers that *appear* available based on his trauma profile but that have been empirically tested and failed. Their attempted use against him is a signature of an adversary working from a shallow profile.

- **Money.** Bribes register as insults. He has lived in safehouses for decades by choice; he has no consumption pattern to satisfy.
- **Sexual leverage.** Honey-trap operations against him are reliably futile. His sexual life is bounded to known individuals and his arousal is conditional on trust to a degree that no operative can fake in short order.
- **Threats to himself.** His own safety has zero leverage value. Threats to his life accelerate compliance only if the threatened death would prevent him completing an obligation; otherwise they are received with equanimity.
- **Ideological appeals.** Patriotism, partisanship, religious framing — all register as institutional manipulation and reduce trust in the speaker.
- **Pharmacological coercion.** He has been pharmacologically manipulated for decades; he has developed both tolerance and a precise vocabulary for the subjective experience. He notices and reports it earlier than non-conditioned subjects would.
- **Public shaming.** His self-condemnation already exceeds anything an external accuser could supply; the marginal effect of public denunciation is approximately zero. Worse: it confirms his self-narrative and entrenches it.

The fact that none of these work narrows the adversary profile considerably. **Anyone who succeeds in moving him against his interests is using one of the load-bearing levers in Sections I–IV, not these.**

---

## VIII. DE-ESCALATION PROTOCOL (Calming Sequence, in Order)

For use by trusted persons during dissociative narrowing, post-action shutdown, or partial trigger activation.

1. **Verbal identification of self and location.** First-person name of the speaker, current location in plain language, current date. Spoken at conversational volume in English. Do not shout. Do not touch first.
2. **Operational summary.** "The objective is complete / the threat is down / we are extracting now." His operational mind will re-engage before his personal mind. Give it something to engage with.
3. **Named-attachment anchor.** Reference to a member of the in-group, by name, with their current status. "Steve is at the rendezvous. Nat is on overwatch. Sam is twenty minutes out." The names function as proof-of-world.
4. **Physical proximity without restraint.** Stand within arm's reach. Do not block egress. Do not approach from behind. Do not restrain him under any circumstances — restraint will worsen the state.
5. **A task.** Once verbal contact is established, give him a small, immediate, defensible task — secure a perimeter, carry a piece of equipment, drive. Re-engagement of operational competence accelerates re-integration.
6. **Do not require disclosure.** He will not describe what happened. Asking him to is counterproductive. The debrief, if it happens, will occur hours or days later, often in writing or in motion (he talks while walking, not while sitting), and should be received without follow-up questions.
7. **Sleep, food, warmth, in that order, within the next twelve hours.** If he refuses, frame each as a mission-readiness requirement, not as care.

---

## IX. PREDICTIVE INDICATORS (Early-Warning Signature)

Behavioral micro-changes that precede larger decompensation, drawn from the longitudinal record. Observers should be trained on the full set.

- **Withdrawal of humor.** The dry, oblique 1940s register thinning out is the earliest indicator. He stops making the small jokes before he stops doing anything else.
- **Verbal economy collapse.** Sentences shorten. Contractions disappear. He begins to answer in fragments. This is two to three days before significant decompensation.
- **Route rigidification.** He has always varied his routes through any environment he uses repeatedly. When the variation stops — when he begins taking the same path two days running — he is conserving cognitive load because something else is consuming it.
- **Increased solo training.** Hours on the range, the mat, the bag, beyond maintenance levels. He is preparing for something he has not announced.
- **Cleaning of weapons he is not currently using.** A displacement ritual, repeatedly noted in the record. He cleans the weapons of his past to manage the present.
- **Refusal of meals taken in company.** He will continue to eat, but alone. The shift from communal to solitary eating is a reliable indicator that the in-group is being placed at protective distance.
- **Reading of his own file.** Anytime he is observed re-reading the Department X material, the Siberian extradition documents, or the Winter Soldier kill list, the next several weeks should be expected to involve self-handicapping volunteer behavior. The reading is a self-administered re-loading of the debt.
- **Letters written and not sent.** Across multiple writers, the depicted habit of composing correspondence — to the dead, to victims, to Rogers in the years Rogers was gone — that is never delivered. Discovery of such drafts in his personal effects indicates that a current event has activated unfinished historical material.

---

## X. THE STRUCTURAL VULNERABILITY (The One That Cannot Be Patched)

Underneath every specific lever above is the single architectural fact from which they all descend: **he will accept his own destruction in the service of the debt, and he does not believe the debt can be cleared.** This means that no protective regime can be built on the assumption that his self-preservation instinct will hold. It will not. It is the variable that an adversary with sufficient patience will eventually find a way to exploit, and it is the variable that his protectors must therefore supply *from outside him* — by valuing his survival on his behalf, refusing missions on his behalf, and, when necessary, lying to him about whether alternatives existed, on his behalf.

The protective community around him is, in effect, his missing self-preservation function. The compendium above is the operating manual for that function. It is to be held by the few, used sparingly, and never weaponized against him by those entrusted with it — because the deepest vulnerability he has is that he has, against everything that was done to him, chosen to trust again, and the integrity of that trust is the load-bearing wall of the entire remaining personality.

Protect the wall.

— END SECTION —


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — SUBJECT BARNES, J.B.

*Asset ledger compiled from operational record 1941–present. Intended as the positive-column inventory: what the subject possesses, what he can deploy, what has kept him alive and morally legible across more than a century of conditions designed to destroy both.*

---

## 1. PHYSICAL & SOMATIC ASSETS

**Baseline physiology.** Subject is the recipient of a partial, non-Erskine variant of the super-soldier process administered by Department X (Karpov-era refinement of stolen American protocols, *Captain America* vol. 5 #11–14; reiterated in *Winter Soldier* solo, Brubaker, 2012). Effects: musculoskeletal output approximately 1.4–1.6× peak human baseline; reaction latency in the 110–130 ms range (measured against Rogers's ~100 ms); injury recovery accelerated roughly 3–4× civilian baseline; resistance to infection, hypothermia, and pharmacological sedation markedly elevated. He does not match Rogers's ceiling and has never tried to; what he possesses is *enough margin to do the job and keep working when wounded.*

**Cryogenic durability.** Repeated freeze-thaw cycles across approximately five decades have, paradoxically, preserved rather than degraded him. Telomeric attrition is functionally arrested during stasis. Biological age held in the third decade. Operational implication: he has another century of useful life if he chooses to spend it.

**The vibranium prosthesis (Wakandan generation).** Neurally integrated via direct interface with brachial plexus remnant; mass approximately 4.8 kg (compared to ~11 kg for the Soviet generation); tensile capacity sufficient to arrest a moving vehicle; vibranium lattice absorbs and re-emits kinetic energy, permitting catch-and-return of high-velocity projectiles including, on documented occasion, Rogers's shield. The arm is electromagnetically shielded, EMP-resistant, and self-diagnosing. *Critical asset value beyond capability: it is the first piece of him that was given as a gift rather than installed as a leash.* The somatic shift from Soviet to Wakandan hardware is the difference between carrying his torturers in his shoulder and carrying his forgivers there. This is durable resilience infrastructure, not merely a weapon.

**Ambidexterity and cross-dominance.** Original right-hand dominance; left-hand function rebuilt from prosthesis upward through forty years of forced training. He now operates symmetrically — can shoot, write, knife-work, and pick locks with either hand. Few human operators on record possess equivalent bilateral parity.

**Sensory acuity.** Conditioning included sustained scotopic and auditory discrimination training; he reads low-light environments at near-cat thresholds and discriminates suppressed-weapon report by manufacturer and caliber. Olfactory recognition of chemical signatures (cordite, specific accelerants, certain solvents) is documented across the Brubaker run.

**Pain tolerance.** Calibrated by both serum effect and conditioning. He has continued mission execution through gunshot, stab, fracture, and electrical injury without observable functional decrement. This is double-edged — it permits him to ignore signal he should heed — but operationally it is an unambiguous asset.

---

## 2. TRADECRAFT & COMBAT CAPABILITIES

**Firearms.** Master-grade proficiency across small arms, carbines, precision rifles, and crew-served weapons of every major manufacturing tradition (American, Soviet/Russian, German, Belgian, Israeli, Chinese). He maintains a personal preference for older, mechanically simpler weapons — visible across runs in his recurrent return to a stripped 1911-pattern sidearm and a bolt-action rifle for precision work — because they are field-serviceable without supply chain. He sights left-handed despite original right-eye dominance, a residue of Department X retraining.

**Edged weapons.** Standout discipline. Throwing-knife work at distances of 8–12 meters with reliable lethal placement; combat knife in CQB rotates between reverse and forward grips fluidly; documented familiarity with karambit, kukri, and Soviet *NR-40* pattern. The blade is his most personal weapon — the one that requires he be present in the moment of killing.

**Unarmed combat.** Hybrid system — original 1930s Brooklyn street boxing (jab-cross-hook lineage, drop-step entry) overlaid with Soviet Systema (joint manipulation, off-balancing, breath-work) and a layer of Wakandan close-quarter forms acquired during the White Wolf rehabilitation period. The result is unorthodox by any single school's standards and therefore difficult to anticipate.

**Sniping.** Confirmed long-range engagements at distances exceeding 1,800 meters under adverse weather. Patience phase — the hours of stillness in a hide — is his native state; he is one of the few operators on record for whom the wait is restful rather than taxing.

**Demolitions and sabotage.** Trained pre-war by Army intelligence for industrial sabotage; updated continuously through Department X and later S.H.I.E.L.D. read-in. Comfortable with improvised, military, and modern shaped-charge inventories. Disproportionately skilled at *non-destructive sabotage* — the kind that looks like component failure rather than attack.

**Languages.** Fluent: English, Russian, German, French. Conversational: Romanian, Mandarin, Arabic, Wakandan (acquired during the Birnin Zana residence). Reading proficiency in Polish, Czech, Korean. Accent control is exceptional — he can pass as native or near-native in at least four of these.

**Surveillance, counter-surveillance, escape and evasion.** Top-tier across the board. Memorized escape routes from any space he sits in for more than ten minutes. Can build a clean identity in a working European city in 72 hours; has demonstrated this repeatedly across the Bucharest period and the post-Thunderbolts solo runs.

**Vehicular.** Rated on rotary-wing, fixed-wing prop, motorcycle (every era from 1940 to present), small watercraft, tracked vehicles. Driving style is economical, defensive, and unflashy — he treats vehicles as cover and movement, not as performance objects.

**Cyber and signals.** Mid-tier by 21st-century standards; competent at operational security, encrypted comms, basic OSINT, but defers to specialists (Romanova, Shuri, Wilson's network) for offensive cyber. Knows what he doesn't know — itself an asset.

---

## 3. COGNITIVE & EXECUTIVE ASSETS

**Operational intelligence.** Tested IQ irrelevant; functional cognition is high-fluid, high-crystallized, with exceptional working memory under stress. He retains mission detail across multi-week timelines without notes and can reconstruct rooms, routes, and conversations after a single exposure.

**Theory of mind.** Sharp and predictive. Reads handlers, targets, and allies accurately and quickly. He clocks deception within seconds and rarely telegraphs that he has. The blind spot is *self*-perception, not other-perception — which means in any room except one containing a mirror, his social intelligence is an unambiguous asset.

**Planning style.** Bounded and modular. He builds plans with explicit failure branches and pre-committed abort criteria. He does not improvise unnecessarily but improvises competently when forced. He plans missions in granular detail and life in days — the second is a deficit but the first is gold.

**Memory architecture, post-restoration.** Counterintuitively a strength. Decades of deliberate memory disruption produced, upon restoration, an unusually *cataloged* memory — he holds his own history in something closer to a case file than a stream, which permits him to inspect specific incidents without being submerged by them. Painful as a way to live; useful as a way to debrief.

**Learning curve.** Acquires new systems — weapons, languages, software, social codes — at a rate consistent with elite-level adult learners. Wakandan period demonstrates this most cleanly: from extracted asset to functional integration in a markedly foreign cultural and technological environment within approximately two years.

---

## 4. MORAL & CHARACTEROLOGICAL ASSETS

**Conscience, intact and load-bearing.** The single most important asset on this ledger. After everything done to him and through him, the moral apparatus survives — bruised, hypertrophied in some directions, but operational. The presence of moral injury (per Griffin et al., 2019) is itself evidence: only an intact conscience can be injured by transgression. He continues to be capable of the distinction between killing and murder, and to act on it.

**Reliability of commitment.** Once he extends trust, he does not retract it casually. Allies report — across decades of writers — that an agreement with Barnes is functionally a contract. He has broken commitments only when keeping them would have required harming the protected party, and even then he has flagged the break in advance where possible.

**Capacity to receive correction.** Notable. When Rogers, Romanova, T'Challa, Shuri, Wilson, or Yelena have pushed back on his choices, he listens. He does not always comply, but he registers. He is not defended against being told he is wrong — partly because he expects to be wrong about himself in the direction of worse than he is.

**Absence of grandiosity.** No messianic strain; no martyrdom theatrics (despite martyrdom-adjacent behavior); no need to be seen doing the work. He will accept anonymous credit for his worst acts and refuse public credit for his best — the inverse of the pattern seen in personality-disordered operators.

**Mentorship capability.** Demonstrated with Yelena Belova and with younger operators in the Thunderbolts roster (Rosenberg run). His teaching style is patient, technical, and undefended — he will narrate his own mistakes as instructional material without flinching. Few elite operators can do this.

---

## 5. RELATIONAL & SOCIAL CAPITAL

This is, by orders of magnitude, the most undervalued column in his own ledger and the most important one in this assessment.

**Steve Rogers.** The primary attachment, but more importantly, the *proof of concept* that close human bonding survived the conditioning. Rogers functions as secure base, superego proxy, and historical witness — the only person on Earth who knew the pre-war Barnes and the post-restoration Barnes and can adjudicate continuity. Asset value: irreplaceable.

**Natasha Romanova.** Co-survivor of Department X, romantic partner across multiple eras, current professional peer. The relationship's non-domestic structure is a deficit from a flourishing-perspective but an asset from a stability-perspective: it is sustainable on terms both of them can hold. She is also the one person who can speak to him in the conditioning's native register without it being weaponized.

**Sam Wilson.** Adopted-into bond, post-Rogers. Wilson is a trained counselor (canonical, pre-Falcon career) and brings to the relationship an actual professional vocabulary for what Barnes carries. Of the inner circle, Wilson is the one most likely to ask the question Barnes will not ask himself.

**T'Challa and Shuri.** Sovereign-level allies who chose to forgive him before he had earned it and to provide the rehabilitation infrastructure (cryostatic stabilization, conditioning extraction protocols developed by Shuri's team) that no other state would have offered. The White Wolf designation is honorific but it is also a *passport* — Wakandan citizenship-adjacent status remains active and constitutes a permanent retreat option of last resort. Asset value: a sovereign-backed safe harbor.

**Yelena Belova.** Younger-sister-coded bond, complicated by Department X overlap. He is one of the few people she trusts; she is one of the few people he allows to needle him.

**Nick Fury.** Professional patron and the chosen first contact post-restoration. Fury offered the structured reintegration role (Man on the Wall, eventually) that gave Barnes a frame for his capabilities that did not require him to be either weapon or symbol.

**Diffuse network.** S.H.I.E.L.D. successor agencies (variably); Wakandan intelligence services; the surviving 1940s Invaders contacts (Namor, residually); the Thunderbolts roster across iterations. He has more functional allies than he behaviorally acknowledges.

---

## 6. MATERIAL & LOGISTICAL ASSETS

**Safehouses.** Documented and inferred: Bucharest (compromised, abandoned); two Brooklyn locations under non-Barnes identities; at least one Eastern European rural retreat; Wakandan-provided residence (standing offer). Pattern: small, austere, multiple egress points, minimal possessions, books present in every one.

**Identity documents.** Multiple working legends across at least four jurisdictions, maintained at varying levels of refresh. Tradecraft permits rapid rebuild if compromised.

**Financial.** Modest. He does not accumulate; he holds enough operating cash in distributed caches to move and resupply. No conspicuous consumption; no real-estate footprint; back-pay from the U.S. Army (a question raised but unresolved in canon) would, if pursued, render him independently wealthy — he has not pursued it.

**Equipment caches.** Geographically distributed, weapons-and-medical-stocked, refreshed on a personal schedule. He could disappear and re-equip within hours from anywhere in the continental U.S. or western Europe.

---

## 7. RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHAT HAS KEPT HIM FUNCTIONAL

These are the load-bearing supports under everything above.

**The pre-trauma personality survived.** The most remarkable single fact in the file. The wisecracking, loyal, competent young man documented in 1941 is detectable, in muted form, in 2024. Seventy years of industrial unmaking produced erasure but not replacement; the substrate proved more durable than the conditioning intended. This is partially constitutional (something in him refused to be fully overwritten) and partially relational (Rogers's recognition of him was a re-installation).

**Sublimation as primary defense.** Mature, adaptive, and unusually well-developed. He has converted aggression and guilt into a sustained channel of pro-social violence. This is not a workaround; it is a coherent life-strategy that produces value for others while metabolizing harm in him. Sublimation of this caliber is rare and is, by itself, the engine of his functioning.

**Refusal of self-medication.** No alcohol abuse, no opioid use, no benzodiazepine reliance, despite obvious access and obvious justification. He does not permit himself the relief — diagnostically concerning in motive, but functionally a resilience factor: he is never impaired, never withdrawing, never compromised by his own coping mechanism.

**Physical discipline.** Daily training maintained across all post-restoration eras. The body is treated as instrument and as accountability practice. Movement regulates him when nothing else will.

**Capacity for stillness.** Rare in trauma-loaded operators. He can sit. He can wait. He can read. The Bucharest period and the Wakandan goat-tending period both demonstrate sustained tolerance for low-stimulation existence — a capacity most combat operators lose and most never recover.

**Reading as regulatory practice.** Across multiple runs he is depicted reading — history, philosophy, fiction. This is not affectation; it is one of the few activities that occupies cognition without engaging threat-detection. Books are part of the resilience inventory.

**Animal contact (Wakandan period).** The goats. Mocked in fandom; clinically significant. Low-demand, non-verbal, non-judgmental relational practice with creatures that did not know what he had been. This was rehabilitative infrastructure and he submitted to it without resistance — itself a sign of capacity.

**Acceptance of help when offered without performance demands.** He cannot ask for help; he can accept it when it arrives without conditions. T'Challa, Shuri, Rogers, and Romanova have all exploited this loophole productively. The loophole exists because the underlying capacity for connection exists.

**Cataloged rather than flooded trauma memory.** As noted above, the iatrogenic structure of his memory permits inspection without submersion. This is unusual and clinically advantageous — most CPTSD presentations involve intrusion he has been spared by the very mechanism that injured him.

**Moral clarity about the past.** He does not equivocate about what was done. He does not minimize it; he does not catastrophize it past its actual shape. The accuracy of his self-historiography (about events, not about culpability) is itself stabilizing — he is not fighting a fog, he is carrying a known weight.

**Time horizon, expanded by survival.** Having lived through and past conditions that should have killed him, he has acquired — quietly, without articulating it — a certain durability of expectation. He does not panic at adverse developments because he has survived worse and remembers surviving worse. This is a form of earned equanimity that no therapy can manufacture.

---

## 8. STRATEGIC SUMMARY — THE ASSET PROFILE

What the subject brings to any situation he enters: elite-tier kinetic capability backed by a vibranium-grade prosthesis and a century of accumulated tradecraft; intact and unusually durable moral apparatus; reliable commitment once extended; a small but extraordinarily high-quality relational network providing both operational support and ongoing rehumanization; a sublimation-based life-strategy that converts his worst history into others' protection; and a substrate personality that refused to be erased by the most systematic erasure program in published canon.

What keeps him going when the deficits should have closed him down: the named people on the list above; the goats and the books and the daily reps; the Wakandan harbor he does not have to use to benefit from knowing it exists; the slow, unfinished, but real shift from *the weapon installed in his shoulder* to *the gift carried there*; and an underlying constitutional stubbornness, present from 1941, that has outlasted every actor who tried to break it.

The asset ledger is, on net, formidable. The chief obstacle to its full deployment is the subject's persistent refusal to credit it. That is a problem for other sections of this file. For this section the finding is clean: this is a high-value, high-integrity, high-durability human asset, and the dossier should be read accordingly.

— END SECTION —


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — SUBJECT: BARNES, J.B.

> *"He doesn't break loud. He breaks the way a load-bearing wall breaks — quietly, structurally, and you only notice when the ceiling comes down."*
> — operational note, derived from cross-run behavioral pattern

The subject does not decompensate the way most trauma-loaded operators decompensate. There is no rage spiral, no bender, no public unraveling, no suicidal gesture aimed at being caught. His failures are interior, lateral, and slow until they are sudden. What follows is the full topology of his collapse: the staged escalation, the discrete failure modes by category, the somatic and behavioral tells at each rung, the conditions that produce each variant, and the post-collapse recovery signature.

---

## 1. THE ESCALATION LADDER — BASELINE TO BREAK

Mapped from longitudinal behavioral record (Brubaker 2005–2012; Remender *Bitter March*; Kot *Winter Soldier: The Bionic Star*; Ewing *New Avengers*; Rosenberg *Thunderbolts* 2023; Cates material). Six rungs. He can occupy any rung for hours, days, or months. Crossings between rungs are usually unannounced; crossings *back down* are slower than crossings up.

### Rung 0 — Operational Baseline
Hypervigilant calm. Dry humor, intermittently deployed and always with a specific target audience (Rogers, Romanova, Wilson, Yelena — almost never strangers). Sleep is poor but managed: he sleeps in two- to three-hour blocks, often sitting up, often with the left side oriented toward the door. Eats functionally, on a schedule; does not graze. Weapons within arm's reach but not on his body in private space. Reads — books, files, dossiers — in his off-hours; this is his self-soothing modality, the closest thing he has to a hobby. Speaks to perhaps five people a week without an operational reason.

**Tell that he is genuinely at baseline:** he will make a small joke about his arm. Self-deprecation about the prosthesis is the surest sign he is regulated; he cannot joke about it when he is not.

### Rung 1 — Compression
Triggered by: accumulating operational tempo, exposure to a Winter Soldier-era artifact (file, photograph, location, surviving victim or victim's family), a Russian word in casual speech, mild restraint (a tight collar, a seatbelt that catches), cold below freezing without prior acclimation. Also: praise, public acknowledgment, or a stranger expressing gratitude.

Behavioral signature: humor goes first. Verbal economy increases by perhaps 40%. Sentences shorten. He stops initiating conversation but still responds. Eye contact remains, but tracking widens — he is now logging exits and bystanders even in safe rooms. Sleep blocks shorten to ninety minutes. He begins to pace at night, a specific pattern: a perimeter walk of whatever structure he is in, recurring at roughly two-hour intervals. He carries the sidearm in the apartment now.

He does not yet recognize this state as a problem. He believes he is "just tired." This is the cheapest rung to intervene at and the rung at which intervention is most often missed.

### Rung 2 — Withdrawal
Triggered by: any direct request for him to be celebrated, photographed, named in dispatches, or thanked; the death or serious injury of any in-group member; the appearance of new evidence about a Winter Soldier-era kill; sustained domestic intimacy without an operational frame to justify it.

Behavioral signature: he goes geographically lateral. He does not flee — he relocates, quietly and competently, to a peripheral space. In the field this is a different bunk; in a shared safehouse it is moving his gear to whatever room is structurally most defensible and emotionally most distant. He stops eating with others. He begins to take meals standing, at counters, in under four minutes. Showers become shorter, the water colder — a documented pattern across multiple runs, consistent with conditioning-era hygiene regimens. He answers questions in three words or fewer. Touch-tolerance collapses: even Romanova's wrist contact, which he ordinarily accepts, will produce a flinch he cannot fully suppress.

He still functions. He still completes the mission. The cost is being paid invisibly.

### Rung 3 — Penance Acquisition
The diagnostic rung. The hinge between manageable and dangerous.

Triggered by: any of the above sustained beyond roughly seventy-two hours, OR a single high-intensity moral-injury aggravator (encountering a relative of a Winter Soldier victim; being forced to harm a non-combatant in the line of duty; receiving the loyalty of someone he believes does not know what he is).

Behavioral signature: he begins to *seek work*. Specifically, he seeks assignments with unfavorable extraction probabilities — the Man-on-the-Wall pattern, the volunteering for the brief no one else will take. He will phrase this in operational language ("I'm the right tool for this") and the language is not insincere; the targeting calculus is real. What is suppressed is that he is also relieving an internal pressure by accepting a risk he believes he deserves. He sleeps less, perhaps ninety minutes total per night. He stops reading for pleasure. He begins to clean weapons compulsively — not maintenance, *cleaning*, the same field-strip and reassembly performed three and four times in succession. He runs perimeter at night even in spaces with active security.

He will deny being unwell if asked. He will deny it with the same flat operational register he uses to brief a kill. This is the rung at which his closest people — Rogers, Romanova — recognize what is happening and begin to triangulate care without naming it, because naming it ends his cooperation.

### Rung 4 — Constriction
He is now operating on what he believes is professionalism and what is in fact a narrowed dissociative band.

Affect flattens almost completely. The dry humor is gone. He does not refuse food but he forgets it for twelve to eighteen hours at a stretch. Sleep collapses to micro-naps — twenty minutes, often during transit. He becomes preternaturally competent in the field: faster, more economical, lower error rate. *This is the trap.* His operators around him read the competence as recovery; it is in fact the deepening. The Winter Soldier-era training surfaces as motor pattern without the dissociative identity-state — he is moving like the asset while remaining cognitively himself, which is the worst of both, because there is no plausible deniability between him and what he is doing.

Touch-tolerance is zero. Restraint of any kind — handcuffs in a sting operation, a medical strap — risks a partial trigger response. Cold becomes acutely aversive *and* compulsively sought: he will turn off the heat in his quarters and sleep in it because he cannot tolerate comfort. The pacing pattern shifts from perimeter to a fixed loop, often a four- or five-step rectangle, performed in low light.

He stops referring to himself with the first person about Winter Soldier acts. Watch the pronouns. "He" creeps back. "When he was active in Berlin in '78." The splitting language is not full dissociation; it is the cognitive scaffolding of someone preparing to attribute upcoming harm to a self he can disown.

### Rung 5 — Collapse
He has two collapse vectors. They are mutually exclusive in any given episode but both are available to him.

**5a. The Sanctioned Suicide.** He accepts or engineers an assignment with an extraction probability he privately assesses near zero. He does this with full operational competence and without melodrama. He briefs the team, writes the contingencies, and walks into the room. If asked directly whether he expects to come back, he will say "we'll see" — a phrase he uses for nothing else, and which is the closest he comes to a goodbye note. The intent is not classically suicidal; it is *settlement*. He is allowing the work to take what he believes the work is owed. The Siberian extradition acceptance (Cap #616 ff., 2011) is the cleanest canonical example: he does not seek death, he simply stops obstructing it. The literature on moral injury (Griffin et al., 2019) predicts exactly this — self-injurious sequelae as restitution, not as despair.

**5b. The Trigger-State Breach.** Under sufficient combined load (Russian phrase-string + restraint + cold + sleep debt > ~96 hours), his learned inhibitory countermeasures fail and a partial Winter Soldier state surfaces. Not the full programmed asset of the Department X era — integration has been deep enough to prevent that in most depictions — but a band of functioning in which his targeting becomes indiscriminate-within-mission-parameters, his speech drops into Russian, and his recognition of in-group members degrades. This is the failure mode he fears most and structures his entire life around preventing. When it happens, post-event, he will not speak for hours; he will surrender his weapons unprompted; he will request restraint (the only context in which he will accept it); he will refuse food until told to eat by Rogers or Romanova specifically.

---

## 2. THE CONDITIONS THAT PRODUCE COLLAPSE

Decompensation in this subject is not random. It is the product of identifiable load profiles. Five distinct precipitant patterns recur across canon.

### 2.1 The Anniversary Load
Calendar-anchored. Specific dates produce predictable Rung 1–2 escalations even in the absence of other stressors: the date of the drone-plane fall (March 1945, per Brubaker dating); the date of his first confirmed Winter Soldier-era kill (the file gives this ambiguously, but his behavior around late autumn is notably worse year over year); Rogers's "death" date during the Civil War aftermath; the dates of specific victims' deaths where families are still living. He does not mark these dates aloud. He marks them by going quieter. A handler tracking him would build a calendar of his silences and find them load-bearing.

### 2.2 The Restoration Cascade
Encounter with material that returns lost memory. Photographs, archival film, files unsealed by FOIA-equivalent processes, surviving witnesses. Each new piece of restored memory is not relief — it is *new debt*. He decompensates after restoration, not before. The pattern is reliable: a quiet 48 hours of intake, then Rung 2 withdrawal, then Penance Acquisition behavior within the week. This is why supervised, paced disclosure is the only ethical method of reintegrating his archival history; uncontrolled disclosure (a journalist's piece, a leak, a hostile actor weaponizing the file) reliably produces Rung 4 within ten days.

### 2.3 The Intimacy Threshold
Sustained domestic relational structure crosses a threshold his nervous system reads as threat. The mechanism is conditioning-derived: under Department X, attachment was the punishment — bonds were permitted and then amputated. His substrate has learned that consolidation of intimacy precedes its violent removal. Therefore he himself dismantles it before it can be dismantled for him.

The threshold is roughly: shared residence beyond three months; shared routine including domestic rituals (meals, mornings, shared sleep schedule); any conversation involving futures longer than the current operational horizon; the introduction of him to an extended social field of the partner (her friends, her family, her civilian life). Cross these and he begins Rung 2 withdrawal within two weeks. The non-domestic structure of the Romanova partnership is not stylistic — it is *protective architecture*, mutually constructed, that has kept the relationship viable for decades by never crossing the threshold.

### 2.4 The Acclamation Event
Public honor, ceremony, medal, named dispatch, photograph in press. Any moment where he is required to stand still and be thanked. The Griffin et al. moral injury literature predicts this: praise for service is intolerable when the self-concept is organized around penance. To accept the praise is to falsify the debt; to refuse the praise publicly is to embarrass the people who organized it. He therefore *removes himself*. Diplomatically when possible. Bluntly when not. A handler who needs him out of a building need only schedule a ceremony in it.

### 2.5 The Coerced Innocent
The single highest-load trigger. Any operation in which he is required, by tactical necessity or systemic constraint, to allow harm to come to a non-combatant — even harm he did not himself execute and could not have prevented — produces a compressed walk through Rungs 1 to 4 in days. This is the cleanest reproduction of the original Winter Soldier-era moral injury structure: harm to the innocent under conditions of constrained agency. The recovery from this precipitant is the slowest of all the listed conditions; canonical depictions show weeks of Rung 3–4 behavior following such an event, with the Penance Acquisition phase often producing the Rung 5a sanctioned-suicide vector.

---

## 3. SOMATIC AND BEHAVIORAL TELLS — A FIELD GUIDE BY RUNG

For anyone responsible for his care or his deployment. Read top to bottom; the appearance of any item from a higher rung in the absence of items from lower rungs is diagnostic of acceleration.

**Sleep.** Baseline: 4–6 hours, fragmented. Rung 1: 3 hours, fragmented, sitting. Rung 2: <2 hours. Rung 3: <90 minutes. Rung 4: micro-naps in transit. Rung 5: he has not slept and does not intend to.

**Speech volume.** Baseline: conversational with in-group, sparing with others. Rung 1: clipped. Rung 2: three words. Rung 3: operational only. Rung 4: monosyllabic. Rung 5a: a single phrase ("we'll see"). Rung 5b: Russian.

**Pronoun usage re: Winter Soldier history.** Baseline: first person ("I killed him in '72"). Rung 3 onward: third person creeps in. By Rung 4 it has displaced first person almost entirely. Rung 5: he no longer references the era at all.

**Left arm.** Baseline: integrated, gestures with it, self-deprecates about it. Rung 2: gestures stop. Rung 3: he begins to keep it close to the body, often resting the flesh hand over the prosthesis at the wrist — the only self-soothing gesture he has. Rung 4: he stops looking at it. Rung 5b: he leads with it.

**Cleaning behavior.** Baseline: routine maintenance, weekly. Rung 3: daily field-strip and reassembly of carry weapons. Rung 4: multiple sequential strips, often the same weapon, performed in low light. The compulsive cleaning is the most visible Rung 3 marker and the one most legible to an outside observer.

**Eating.** Baseline: scheduled, functional, with others when offered. Rung 2: alone, standing, under four minutes. Rung 3: forgotten for half-day stretches, eaten in single sittings of high caloric density. Rung 4: ignored entirely; will eat only when told by a specific person.

**Temperature regulation.** Baseline: indifferent to ambient. Rung 3: heat off in personal quarters. Rung 4: he is cold and is choosing to be cold and will not name it.

**Touch.** Baseline: accepts contact from in-group, withdraws from strangers. Rung 2: flinches at in-group contact. Rung 4: zero tolerance, including incidental contact. Rung 5b: contact is read as threat.

**Pacing pattern.** Baseline: none. Rung 1: perimeter walks at two-hour intervals. Rung 4: a fixed small loop, often a four- or five-step rectangle, in low light, repeated to the point of wear in flooring.

**Self-deprecating arm joke.** Present at Baseline. Absent by Rung 1. The earliest reliable tell.

---

## 4. WHAT HIS COLLAPSE DOES *NOT* LOOK LIKE

The decompensation profile of this subject is so consistently misread by outsiders that the negative space is itself diagnostic. He does not:

- **Drink.** The absence of alcohol use is itself a symptom — he denies himself the standard self-medication route because the relief would falsify the debt. Anyone observing him drinking heavily should consider impersonation, coercion, or radical breakthrough rather than relapse.
- **Rage.** He has no outward anger phase. Frustration sinks rather than vents. A subject who shouts at his team is not this subject in collapse — it is this subject performing for a reason.
- **Self-harm visibly.** No cutting, no overt suicidal gesture, no overdose. His self-harm is always *mission-channeled* — the sanctioned suicide of Rung 5a. To intervene effectively, one must recognize that an operational decision is functioning as self-harm.
- **Confess.** He does not unburden. He does not give a long-form account of his suffering to a trusted other under pressure. Confession would be relief, and relief is contraindicated by his self-concept. The handful of canonical scenes where he does speak at length are extracted, not offered.
- **Run.** He does not abandon post or disappear into civilian anonymity. Even in his deepest withdrawal he remains reachable by the in-group through known channels. The withdrawal is *lateral, not absent.*
- **Sleep too much.** Depressive hypersomnia is not in his repertoire. His depressive load expresses as insomnia and constriction, not collapse into bed.
- **Lose competence.** Right up to Rung 5 his operational capacity is preserved or even sharpened. This is the most dangerous feature of his decompensation pattern — *functioning is preserved while structure fails.* He is the load-bearing wall.

---

## 5. RECOVERY SIGNATURE

Re-compensation, when it happens, is slower than decompensation by roughly a factor of three. Days down, weeks up. The sequence is reliable and runs in reverse order of the rung tells, with one inversion.

The first recovery marker is not the return of speech or appetite. It is the return of *reading*. When he picks up a book again — not a file, a book — he has crossed back below Rung 3. Then sleep extends. Then he resumes shared meals, though he will still take them quickly. Then touch-tolerance returns to in-group only. Then the pronouns shift back to first person. Then, last, the self-deprecating arm joke returns. When that joke returns, he is back at Baseline.

The recovery cannot be rushed. Attempts to accelerate it — by reassurance, by celebration of his return, by any public acknowledgment of what he has been through — push him back up the ladder. The correct intervention is presence without demand: Rogers reading in the same room without speaking; Romanova sharing a safehouse without converting it to a home; Wilson handing him a task he can complete in an afternoon. Care delivered as work he can accept rather than as kindness he must metabolize.

---

## 6. CATASTROPHIC FAILURE — THE WORST-CASE PROFILE

The single condition under which this subject's normal collapse architecture breaks down entirely:

**Loss of Rogers.**

Every other failure mode he has rehearsed and contains some adaptation to. The Rogers bond is the superego proxy and the secure base both; it is the operator on which "what would Steve do" runs, and it is the anchor that keeps his self-concept from sliding into pure instrument. Canonical evidence: when Rogers was assassinated, Barnes accepted the shield *only* because the mantle was framed as Rogers's posthumous wish. The mantle was not recovery — it was a coffin he carried for three years.

A permanent loss of Rogers without that posthumous framing — without the explicit transmitted instruction — would produce, predictably:

1. Compressed walk through Rungs 1–4 within 96 hours.
2. Rung 5a engagement (sanctioned suicide vector) within two weeks, masked as operational necessity.
3. If 5a is blocked by external intervention (Romanova, Wilson, Wakandan custodial care), Rung 4 constriction sustained indefinitely, with secondary depressive features becoming clinically primary.
4. Risk of Rung 5b (trigger-state breach) elevated permanently due to loss of the highest-order inhibitory anchor.

Mitigating factor: Romanova and Wilson can hold the secondary anchor position. Yelena and Shuri tertiary. The in-group is small but it is genuinely a network, not a single point of failure. He has built it — slowly, through the 2010s and into the 2020s material — as the only architecture he trusts: not redemption, but redundancy.

---

## 7. SUMMARY — THE STRUCTURE OF HIS BREAKING

He breaks the way structures designed to absorb load break. Not through fracture but through accumulating microdeformation, until a final stressor crosses the elastic limit and what looked like the same wall it always was is suddenly carrying no weight at all. The competence is preserved through the failure. The voice is preserved. The targeting is preserved. What fails is the part of him that distinguishes between the man and the weapon, and when that fails he chooses, consistently and without melodrama, to point the weapon at something that he has decided deserves to receive it — including, when the math runs that way, himself.

The intervention window is narrow and is located early: Rungs 1 and 2, when the arm joke is gone and the pacing has started and no one has yet said the word *thank you* in a room he cannot leave. After Rung 3 the cost of intervention rises steeply. After Rung 4 the only intervention that works is the physical presence of a named other, sustained, silent, and undemanding, for as long as it takes for him to pick up a book.

— END SECTION —


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — SUBJECT: BARNES, J. B.

*Prepared by UATU, Watcher-designate. Section VII of dossier. This section forecasts; it does not determine. Where the prior sections mapped what the subject is and has been, this section maps the vector — where the arc is currently pointing, what would bend it, and what would break it.*

---

## 1. THE BASELINE EXTRAPOLATION (the "do-nothing" trajectory)

If no novel stressor and no novel intervention enter the system in the next decade of his subjective life, the subject continues exactly as he is. This is not stagnation; it is a stable equilibrium maintained by constant work. He will:

- Maintain a small fixed-cost life — one apartment, kept sparsely; two or three safehouses he refreshes on a rotation; a go-bag he repacks the first Sunday of every month whether it needs it or not.
- Continue mission-cycling: an operational tempo of roughly one high-risk assignment every five-to-nine weeks, calibrated to keep his moral ledger appearing to move without requiring him to confront whether it ever can.
- Maintain his three-to-four-person inner circle with steady, undemonstrative contact: a check-in call to Rogers most weeks, a coffee-or-knife-cleaning evening with Romanova on no fixed schedule but reliably, a text-thread with Wilson that is mostly memes returned with one-word answers, occasional contact with Yelena that he initiates more often than the file would predict.
- Sleep four-to-five hours per night, broken into two shifts; pace the perimeter of whatever space he is in between them; not name this as insomnia even to himself.
- Refuse three offers of leadership for every one he accepts under coercion.

This baseline is sustainable for years. It is not, however, sustainable indefinitely. The mathematical fact of the equilibrium is that it requires the input variable — *missions on which to expend the debt* — to remain available at constant rate. The world will not cooperate. There will be lulls. The lulls are the danger.

---

## 2. THE OPEN QUESTIONS (the file's unresolved variables)

Six questions the case officer cannot yet answer; each is a fork.

**Q1 — Whether he is capable of accepting a future tense for himself.** Across canon he plans missions in operational detail and life in days. The question is not whether he can imagine a future (he can; he is not concretely suicidal) but whether he can imagine a future *with himself in it as a person* rather than as an instrument. Every depicted attempt at domesticity has aborted. The question remains live.

**Q2 — Whether the trigger substrate is degrading, stable, or rebuildable.** The Wakandan deprogramming demonstrably reduced trigger-cue reactivity but did not abolish the conditioned pathway. We do not know if twenty more years of disuse will erode it further, if it is now stable at residual baseline, or if a sufficiently determined adversary with a new Winter Soldier protocol could re-cut the channel. He does not know either. He carries the uncertainty as a low-grade background hum.

**Q3 — Whether Rogers's presence is, on net, anchor or arrest.** Rogers stabilizes him. Rogers also functions as the superego proxy that prevents him from constructing an internal superego of his own. As long as the moral operator "what would Steve do" is available, he does not have to develop the operator "what do *I* think is right." This works while Rogers is present and reachable. The question is what happens the next time Rogers is not.

**Q4 — Whether the Romanova relationship will resolve toward intimacy or remain in operational equipoise.** Currently a stable non-domestic partnership that functions because both parties tacitly refuse to escalate. Both have the structural capacity to escalate. Neither has the structural capacity to be the one who asks first. The question is whether anything ever forces the issue, and how each responds.

**Q5 — Whether the moral injury will integrate, calcify, or perforate.** Three possible long-term courses for the moral-injury substrate: *integration* (he comes to hold the Winter Soldier acts as things that happened to a body he was inside without electing to be, while remaining motivated by the wish to do better — Griffin et al.'s best-outcome trajectory); *calcification* (he stabilizes around the present penance model indefinitely, which is functional but costly); *perforation* (a single event — a victim's family confronting him, a recovered memory of a specific kill — punches through the current containment and triggers a crisis). All three remain possible.

**Q6 — Whether he will ever permit himself to be cared for in a register that is not earned.** The Wakandan period was the closest approach. He accepted Shuri's medical attention; he accepted Okoye's drills; he accepted T'Challa's hospitality. He accepted all of it as work — as something he was doing in exchange for the deprogramming. Whether he can ever accept care simply as care is unknown.

---

## 3. THE FORK POINTS (where the trajectory will bifurcate)

These are the events — none certain, all plausible within the established universe — at which the case will branch. The dossier flags each with its growth-vector and its catastrophe-vector.

### Fork A — A definitive loss of Rogers.

Rogers has died, returned, aged out, returned, been replaced by Wilson, and resumed in various permutations. The next time Rogers is *durably* removed from the board (death without recovery; permanent retirement to an inaccessible state; cognitive decline), the subject loses his superego proxy.

- *Growth vector:* in the absence of the proxy, the subject is forced to internalize the moral operator. He builds a Steve-shaped function inside himself and over five-to-ten years discovers it has become his own. He emerges with an internal compass not borrowed from a dead man. This is the slow, hard path and it has a real probability — Wilson and Romanova would functionally midwife it.
- *Catastrophe vector:* he experiences the loss as a withdrawal of license-to-exist. The penance loop accelerates. He volunteers for an assignment with negative expected return and executes it with sufficient competence that he survives and is given another. The arc terminates in a Man-on-the-Wall-style fatal mission that everyone present will, with regret, call a hero's death and that the file will record as the slow suicide it was.

### Fork B — A new Winter Soldier program surfaces.

The published universe has repeatedly recapitulated Department X-style asset programs (the Red Room reboots, the Power Broker arc, HYDRA remnants, the Thunderbolts framing). The next time one surfaces, the subject will be drawn in — as advisor, as bait, as rescuer of the new conditioned assets.

- *Growth vector:* he becomes the person he needed at twenty-eight. He mentors a generation of deprogrammed assets, structures a methodology, allows himself to be *useful in a register that is not lethality*. The mentorship of Yelena is the prototype; the program would be the maturation. This is the trajectory in which his expertise becomes a gift rather than a wound.
- *Catastrophe vector:* exposure to the conditioning environment in a sustained way reactivates the trigger substrate. He performs the rescue, frees the assets, and finds that he himself is partially re-shaped by the proximity. He withdraws further; he begins to doubt the integration he has achieved; the recovery work of twenty years partially undoes.

### Fork C — A victim's family.

A surviving family member of a Winter Soldier kill locates him and confronts him. Canon has flirted with this but not committed; the case officer regards it as a near-certain eventual event given the number of kills and the public knowledge of his identity.

- *Growth vector:* he receives the confrontation, does not flinch, offers no defense, accepts whatever the surviving family asks of him short of self-destruction — testimony, financial restitution, public acknowledgment, his physical presence at a grave. The encounter discharges some of the diffuse shame into specific repair. He emerges marginally lighter.
- *Catastrophe vector:* the surviving family asks for his death and he agrees with them. He does not act on it immediately; he carries the agreement inward and it metastasizes. Within six months he is dead by a mission he engineered to look operational.

### Fork D — A child.

He is placed, by circumstance, in protracted custodial responsibility for a child — a survivor of an operation he ran; an orphan of the Red Room; Yelena's responsibility transferred temporarily. He has no canonical paternity history and has avoided the position structurally.

- *Growth vector:* the parentified-orphan substrate inverts. The child elicits competencies he did not know he had retained — patience, playfulness, the warmth that the 1940s persona carried before it was amputated. He discovers that the original Bucky was not destroyed, only buried, and that a small person calling for him in the night can reach what no adult could. This is the highest-trajectory outcome in the entire forecast space and also the one he would most resist arranging deliberately.
- *Catastrophe vector:* the child is harmed on his watch, by adversaries targeting him. He survives the recovery; he does not survive the moral weight. This becomes the perforating event under Q5.

### Fork E — The triggering of a final, irrecoverable memory.

He has cumulative memory restoration but the file assesses, on the basis of the depicted gaps, that some kills remain unmemoried. The next is the worst — a child, a friend's relative, a victim whose identity collapses a load-bearing relationship.

- *Growth vector:* he tells someone. Romanova, Rogers, Wilson, his therapist if Wakanda assigned one (the file suspects they did and he attends sporadically). The mere act of speaking it into another person's hearing prevents the perforation.
- *Catastrophe vector:* he does not tell anyone. He absorbs it alone and recalibrates his sense of what he owes. The penance accelerates without anyone around him knowing why.

### Fork F — Offered a normal life by someone who will not take refusal as the final answer.

The dossier flags this as the single most destabilizing possible event, per Section 4's pressure-point analysis. It has been tried — Rogers, in soft form; the Wakandan offer of permanent residence; Romanova in periodic implicit form — and refused each time. The next offer comes from someone whose refusal-tolerance is lower.

- *Growth vector:* he accepts a constrained version. Not retirement, not domesticity in full, but a *reduction of the operational tempo from every six weeks to every six months,* with the intervening time spent at a single address with a person who knows what he is. The reduction is enough. The body and mind begin to recover what constant tempo prevented.
- *Catastrophe vector:* the offer triggers acute distress; he disappears; he reappears on a mission he should not have taken; the cycle reasserts at higher intensity than before.

---

## 4. WHAT WOULD PUSH HIM TOWARD GROWTH

Catalogued as discrete interventions, in descending order of expected effect. None are sufficient alone; the combination is what would move the needle.

**(a) A therapeutic relationship he does not control.** He will accept a clinician if assigned by someone he trusts (Shuri, hypothetically; Wilson, if framed as a condition of continued team membership). He will use the relationship if the clinician is uninterested in his fame, unimpressed by his history, and willing to sit with long silences. The Wakandan team likely structured this; whether he has continued it outside that context is the open file item. Continuation is the single highest-leverage intervention available.

**(b) Sustained low-stakes social ritual.** Not therapy, not mission debriefs — a weekly poker game, a standing breakfast, a recurring obligation to be in a room with people who expect nothing from him beyond presence. The dossier's behavioral record suggests he will resist initiating but will not abandon once established. Wilson is the most likely architect.

**(c) Bodily care he is forced to accept.** Physical therapy on the shoulder articulation; sleep medicine; nutrition that is not field-rations. Each requires him to attend to the body as something other than a tool. Each is small. The accumulation matters.

**(d) Mentorship duties that are not transferable.** A protégé he cannot delegate. The presence of a person whose development depends on him forces him into a future tense — you cannot mentor someone if you do not plan to be alive next year.

**(e) An act of restitution that he chooses.** Not assigned penance — chosen repair. A foundation funded in the name of victims; testimony given at a tribunal; sustained quiet work on a problem he selects because it matters to him rather than because it was handed to him. The shift from imposed to elected penance is the shift from moral injury active to moral injury integrating.

**(f) Permission, from a source he cannot dismiss, to feel a positive affect.** The hardest. Likely arrives, if it arrives, from a child or from Romanova in an unguarded moment. Cannot be engineered; can only be recognized when it appears.

---

## 5. WHAT WOULD PUSH HIM TOWARD CATASTROPHE

In descending order of severity.

**(a) Re-conditioning.** Capture by a successor program with current neurotechnology and time. The file estimates partial re-shaping is achievable in weeks; full reversion is achievable in months. Recovery from a second cycle would be harder than recovery from the first because his current self-narrative includes the belief that he is already past the worst, and the violation of that belief would be its own injury.

**(b) Loss of the entire inner circle in a compressed timeframe.** Sequential or simultaneous removal of Rogers, Romanova, and Wilson within eighteen months. The trust-architecture cannot rebuild that fast. He would not survive it intact; whether he would survive it at all depends on whether Yelena and Shuri reach him in the gap.

**(c) Public legal proceedings without protection.** Extradition or tribunal in a venue that frames him as primarily perpetrator rather than primarily victim, conducted in his absence of strong advocacy. He would not resist; he would accept; the acceptance would be terminal in form even if not in fact.

**(d) Sustained operational idleness.** The world goes quiet. The missions stop. The penance loop has no input. He has no constructed life to fall back on because he has refused to construct one. This is the silent killer — no event, just absence — and it is the form of catastrophe the case officer rates most likely if no growth-vector interventions are made.

**(e) An ally's betrayal.** A member of the inner circle revealed to have been operating against him, or against the values the circle represents, in a way that retroactively recodes a load-bearing relationship. He would not retaliate; he would simply revise downward his estimate of how many people in the world can be trusted, and the revised number would be small enough to be operationally fatal.

**(f) Discovery that a kill he believed conditioned was, in fact, an act in which he retained some agency.** The file flags this as possible per the Brubaker-era depictions of partial lucidity during certain operations. A recovered memory of having *chosen,* in some attenuated sense, would collapse the entire current organizing narrative. This is the perforation under Q5 in its most lethal form.

---

## 6. THE LONG ARC — TEN, TWENTY, FIFTY YEARS

The file is required to project at horizons most case officers refuse. The Watcher does not refuse.

**Ten years out (subjective).** Most probable: stable continuation of present pattern, with marginal reduction in operational tempo as the inner circle's collective gravity slowly draws him toward more time at rest. One major fork-point will likely have triggered (B, C, or F). His residence is likely still mostly Brooklyn-adjacent; he likely owns a dog by year four and will not have named it anything sentimental; he has likely accepted one civilian role (consulting, instruction, advisory) that he characterizes as work but that functions as community.

**Twenty years out.** The Rogers question (Fork A) has resolved one way or the other. If growth-vector: he is the elder of his cohort, the one the younger operators come to for the quiet conversation no one else can have with them, and he has — without announcement — become the person he once needed. If catastrophe-vector: the file is closed.

**Fifty years out.** Conditional on growth-vector resolution of the prior forks: he is still alive, biologically held in early middle age by the residual effects of the cryostatic cycles, increasingly anachronistic, increasingly quiet, increasingly the last living memory of a war no one else remembers. He has likely returned to Brooklyn permanently. He visits graves on a schedule. He has, at some point, stopped counting the debt — not because he decided it was paid but because he forgot, for a week, to check the ledger, and then did not resume. This is the only ending the file regards as fully recovered, and it is achievable.

---

## 7. THE CASE OFFICER'S BOTTOM LINE

The subject is not a man heading toward a crisis. He is a man already inside one, perpetually, who has constructed an equilibrium so competent that observers mistake it for resolution. The equilibrium will hold for as long as the inputs hold. The inputs will not hold forever.

The question that determines everything downstream is whether, in the interval before the equilibrium fails, the people around him succeed in building him a *second* life — a structure of relationships, rituals, and small unearned goods sufficient to catch him when the mission-cycle stops. Rogers cannot build this alone; Rogers is part of the old structure. Romanova will not build it because she shares the pathology. Wilson is building it, slowly, in the form of insistent ordinary friendship. Yelena is building it accidentally by needing him. Shuri built the foundation and handed him the keys.

Whether he uses the keys is the file's central open question. The Watcher's assessment, derived from eighty years of behavioral evidence: *he will, eventually, and later than would be optimal, and the moment will not be marked by any decision he announces, and he will not realize for some time afterward that he has crossed over.*

The dossier is held open pending further developments.

— END SECTION VII —
